# CLAUDE.md

This file provides guidance to Claude Code (claude.ai/code) when working with code in this repository.

## Project Overview

DINOCO System is a **WordPress-based motorcycle warranty management platform** serving B2C members and B2B distributors. All code is PHP executed within WordPress ‚Äî there is no separate build step, no Node.js, and no modern JS framework.

## Architecture

- **Backend**: WordPress + Advanced Custom Fields (ACF). Data is stored in Custom Post Types (claims, registrations, B2B orders) and user metadata.
- **Frontend**: Vanilla HTML/CSS/JavaScript embedded inline in PHP files. UI is exposed via WordPress shortcodes.
- **Authentication**: LINE Login (OAuth2) creates/links WordPress users. Admin access uses `current_user_can('manage_options')`.
- **AI Module (WordPress)**: Google Gemini API with function calling (v22.0). The AI retrieves real data via PHP functions rather than generating answers from training data. Temperature 0.35.
- **AI Module (Chatbot)**: OpenClaw Mini CRM ‚Äî Gemini 2.5 Flash (primary) + Claude Haiku 4.5 (fallback) + Claude Sonnet 4 (supervisor). ýπÑý∏°ýπàý∏°ý∏µ message cap (context ýπÉý∏äýπâ 6-10 messages ý∏•ýπàý∏≤ý∏™ý∏∏ý∏î). Temperature 0.3 (tools), 0.2 (Claude), 0.4 (claim questions).
- **Integrations**: LINE push notifications (B2B alerts), PDF generation (claims), CSV export (admin dashboards).

## REST API Endpoints

**334 register_rest_route calls across 12 namespaces** (verified by Round 30 census `docs/audit/REST-ENDPOINT-CENSUS-2026-04-30.md`, supersedes April-17 audit's 125+ claim). Breakdown: `/b2b/v1/` 128 (84 POST + 44 GET) + `/dinoco-stock/v1/` 42 + `/dinoco-mcp/v1/` 32 + `/b2f/v1/` 29 + `/dinoco-b2f-audit/v1/` 22 + `/dinoco/v1/` 22 + `/dinoco-slip/v1/` 15 + `/liff-ai/v1/` 13 + `/dinoco-flash-golive/v1/` 10 + `/dinoco-gdpr/v1/` 10 + `/brand-voice/v1/` 7 + `/dinoco-export/v1/` 4. Total POST endpoints: **193** (idempotency-coverage denominator). Detailed per-namespace list below.

## REST API Endpoints (B2F Migration Audit ‚Äî Phase 1 + Phase 2)

All under `/wp-json/dinoco-b2f-audit/v1/` (V.2.0 ‚Äî Phase 1 observe-only + Phase 2 Shadow-Write controls):

Phase 1 (observe-only):

- `GET /drift` ‚Äî orphan SETs per maker (SET ý∏óý∏µýπà maker ýπÅý∏ïý∏∞ýπÅý∏ïýπàýπÑý∏°ýπàýπÑý∏îýπâ register)
- `GET /stale?days=90` ‚Äî stale mp_unit_cost records
- `GET /parity/{maker_id}` ‚Äî per-maker parity snapshot
- `GET /dry-run[?preview=1]` ‚Äî trigger + CSV download (or preview JSON)
- `GET /feature-flags` ‚Äî read flags + phase state (schema_activated, backfill_state, table existence)

Phase 2 (V.2.0 Shadow-Write controls):

- `POST /activate-schema` ‚Äî dbDelta canonical tables (`dinoco_product_makers` + `dinoco_maker_product_observations`). Requires `confirm=true`. Calls `b2f_audit_activate_schema_v10()` (database-expert helper). Returns 501 `not_implemented` ý∏ñýπâý∏≤ helper ý∏¢ý∏±ý∏áýπÑý∏°ýπà sync.
- `POST /backfill` ‚Äî ý∏£ý∏±ý∏ô `scripts/b2f-phase2-backfill.php`. Params: `{ confirm: bool, dry_run: bool }`. Persists state to `b2f_phase2_backfill_state` option (ran_at, cpt_migrated, orphans_added, errors, elapsed_ms, uid). Dry-run ýπÑý∏°ýπà save state. Returns 501 ý∏ñýπâý∏≤ script ý∏¢ý∏±ý∏áýπÑý∏°ýπà sync.
- `GET /backfill-status` ‚Äî read last run summary + junction count + schema activation flag
- `POST /feature-flags/toggle` ‚Äî toggle whitelist flag (Phase 2 = ýπÄý∏âý∏ûý∏≤ý∏∞ `b2f_flag_shadow_write`). Guard: ý∏ïýπâý∏≠ý∏áý∏°ý∏µ schema + backfill ý∏Åýπàý∏≠ý∏ôýπÄý∏õý∏¥ý∏î shadow_write. Auto log ý∏úýπàý∏≤ý∏ô `b2f_log_flag_change()` (Snippet 1 V.6.5)
- `GET /junction-snapshot?maker_id=&status=&limit=50` ‚Äî read recent rows + summary (total/active/discontinued/cpt_count/diff_vs_cpt)
- `GET /observations?diff_only=1&maker_id=&limit=50` ‚Äî read recent diff observations + summary (total/diffs/last_24h)

Option F Hybrid Admin Control (V.3.2, 2026-04-16):

- `GET /maker-products-with-source/{maker_id}` ‚Äî junction rows enriched with `source` (`cpt` if `legacy_cpt_id > 0`, else `auto`) + `is_auto_synced` + `is_blacklisted`. Summary { total, cpt, auto, blacklisted }. Used by Admin Makers tab for source badges (üì¶ CPT / ‚ú® Auto)
- `POST /junction-bulk-delete` ‚Äî body `{ maker_id, skus[], add_to_blacklist, only_auto_synced, confirm }`. Soft-delete (status=discontinued, deleted_at=NOW). Default `only_auto_synced=true` ‚Üí SQL WHERE guard `(legacy_cpt_id IS NULL OR legacy_cpt_id=0)` protects CPT rows even if FE bypassed. Rate limit 5/min/user. Returns { deleted, blacklisted, skipped_cpt_protected, errors, updated_blacklist_count }
- `POST /autosync-blacklist` ‚Äî body `{ maker_id, sku, action: 'add'|'remove' }`. Returns updated list + total count
- `GET /autosync-blacklist` ‚Äî full viewer. Returns { blacklist, enriched[] with maker_name, total_entries, size_bytes, cap_bytes=102400 }

### B2F Migration Audit (Phase 1 observe + Phase 2 Shadow-Write)

- **[Admin System] B2F Migration Audit** V.3.3 ‚Äî shortcode `[b2f_migration_audit]`, REST namespace `/wp-json/dinoco-b2f-audit/v1/`. V.3.2 adds Option F Hybrid Admin Control (4 new endpoints + 5 blacklist helpers + `b2f_phase2_run_backfill()` STEP 3 blacklist gate). **V.3.3 (V.7.0 Order Intent)**: Phase 4 migration inline `b2f_phase4_run_classification_migration($dry_run, $batch)` 7-step pipeline (lock flag ‚Üí MySQL check ‚Üí mysqldump snapshot ‚Üí ALTER idempotent ‚Üí classification loop ‚Üí state JSON ‚Üí clear lock). **4 new REST endpoints**: `POST /junction-update-classification` (optimistic concurrency), `POST /junction-bulk-update-display` (max 200 SKUs + idempotency_key), `POST /junction-confirm-classification` (idempotent re-confirm), `POST /phase4-migration` (5/hr rate limit + CSV dry-run export). **Dashboard UI**: "Phase 4 Controls" section (MySQL capability card + state card + dry-run/live buttons + 3 flag toggle rows with dependency chain enforcement). **Flag guards**: `order_intent=ON` requires `v11_explicit_mode=ON`; `ungroup_auto_hide=ON` requires `phase4_migration.finished_at`
- **Purpose**: Option F Hybrid Shadow-Write ‚Äî Phase 1 observability + Phase 2 schema activation/backfill/dual-write enable (ý∏îý∏π `B2F-ARCHITECTURE-PLAN.md`)
- **Feature flags** (wp_options, all default=false): `b2f_flag_auto_sync_sets` (Phase 2.5 locked), `b2f_flag_shadow_write` (Phase 2 toggleable via V.2.0), `b2f_flag_read_from_junction` (Phase 3 locked)
- **Flag helpers** (B2F Snippet 1 V.6.5): `b2f_is_flag_enabled($name)`, `b2f_get_all_flags()`, `b2f_log_flag_change($flag, $old, $new, $uid)` ‚Äî whitelist enforced
- **State helpers** (V.2.0): `b2f_audit_is_schema_activated()`, `b2f_audit_phase2_toggleable_flags()`, `b2f_audit_get_backfill_state()`, `b2f_audit_set_backfill_state()`, `b2f_audit_junction_table_exists()`, `b2f_audit_observations_table_exists()`
- **Dashboard sections** (V.2.0): Phase 2 Controls (3 steps ‚Äî Activate Schema / Run Backfill / Enable Shadow-Write) / Parity Overview / Orphan SETs / Stale Alerts / Feature Flags Panel (toggleable per whitelist) / Junction Snapshot viewer (filter by maker+status) / Diff Observations viewer (filter diff_detected) / Dry-Run Export / 7-day drift history
- **Safety UX**: confirmation dialogs ý∏óý∏∏ý∏Å destructive action / rate limit 5/hr for activate+backfill (reuse `b2b_rate_limit`) / guard shadow_write enable ý∏ïýπâý∏≠ý∏áý∏°ý∏µ schema+backfill ý∏Ñý∏£ý∏öý∏Åýπàý∏≠ý∏ô
- **Database-expert interface** (parallel coordination): endpoints wire ýπÄý∏Çýπâý∏≤ý∏Åý∏±ý∏ö `b2f_audit_activate_schema_v10()` + `scripts/b2f-phase2-backfill.php` ‚Äî ý∏ñýπâý∏≤ helpers ý∏¢ý∏±ý∏áýπÑý∏°ýπà sync ‚Üí endpoint return 501 `not_implemented` + UI ýπÅý∏àýπâý∏áý∏ßýπàý∏≤ "ý∏£ý∏≠ database-expert commit"
- **Reference**: `B2F-ARCHITECTURE-PLAN.md` (Option F plan 4 phases), `B2F-SCHEMA-V10.sql` (canonical schema)

### Canonical B2F Tables (Phase 2 ‚Äî created on Activate Schema)

- `wp_dinoco_product_makers` ‚Äî canonical junction (product_sku √ó maker_id √ó pricing/MOQ/shipping/status/notes + legacy_cpt_id + audit columns + soft delete). Composite unique `uq_sku_maker`, idx_maker_status hot path, idx_legacy_cpt reverse lookup for rollback. utf8mb4_bin on product_sku (case-sensitive UPPER pattern match).
- `wp_dinoco_maker_product_observations` ‚Äî shadow-write diff log (observed_at, source [cpt|junction|diff], sku, maker_id, field_name, cpt_value, junction_value, diff_detected). 60-day TTL via cron `b2f_observations_ttl_cron` (Snippet 11 V.2.2+). Peak ~110K rows = ~50MB.
- Schema marker: `b2f_schema_version` = '10.1', `b2f_schema_v10_activated` = timestamp.

## REST API Endpoints (Flag Audit ‚Äî `dinoco/v1`)

All under `/wp-json/dinoco/v1/flag-audit*` (V.1.0 ‚Äî `[Admin System] DINOCO Flag Audit Log`):

- `GET /flag-audit` ‚Äî list with filters (flag, source, user_id, days, from, to, limit, offset, orderby, order). Returns rows + meta { total, limit, offset, flags[] for distinct dropdown }.
- `GET /flag-audit/{id}` ‚Äî single row detail.
- `POST /flag-audit/retention/run` ‚Äî manual cron trigger (admin only). Returns deleted count + last_run state.
- `GET /flag-audit/export` ‚Äî CSV download (UTF-8 BOM, 5K row cap, `flag` + `days` filter).
- Permission: `manage_options` only. Schema `wp_dinoco_flag_audit` (lazy install on first admin_init).

## REST API Endpoints (Idempotency Helper ‚Äî `dinoco/v1`)

All under `/wp-json/dinoco/v1/idempotency*` (V.1.1 ‚Äî `[Admin System] DINOCO Idempotency Helper`):

- `GET /idempotency` ‚Äî list with filters (namespace, user_id, days, limit, offset). Returns rows + meta.
- `POST /idempotency/cleanup` ‚Äî manual cleanup trigger (admin only). Returns deleted count.
- Permission: `manage_options` + `wp_rest` nonce. Schema `wp_dinoco_idempotency_keys` (lazy install on first admin_init).
- Cleanup cron `dinoco_idempotency_cleanup_cron` registered via `dinoco_register_cron` (Round 28, V.1.1) for Health Monitor heartbeat tracking.
- Used by **28 integrated endpoints** (Rounds 19-28, ~37% of POST surface) ‚Äî see `docs/audit/IDEMPOTENCY-COVERAGE.md` for full tracker:
  - **Round 19** (3): `POST /b2b/v1/place-order`, `POST /b2b/v1/manual-flash-create`, `POST /b2f/v1/create-po`
  - **Round 23** (5): `POST /b2b/v1/confirm-order`, `POST /b2b/v1/flash-create`, `POST /b2b/v1/manual-flash-cancel`, `POST /b2f/v1/po-update`, `POST /b2f/v1/receive-goods`
  - **Round 25** (5): `POST /b2b/v1/update-status`, `POST /b2b/v1/cancel-request`, `POST /b2f/v1/po-cancel`, `POST /b2f/v1/maker-confirm`, `POST /b2f/v1/record-payment`
  - **Round 26** (5): `POST /b2b/v1/bo-confirm-full`, `POST /b2b/v1/bo-split`, `POST /b2b/v1/bo-undo-split`, `POST /b2f/v1/maker-deliver`, `POST /liff-ai/v1/lead/{id}/accept`
  - **Round 27** (5): `POST /b2b/v1/bo-cancel-item`, `POST /b2b/v1/bo-bulk-fulfill`, `POST /b2b/v1/bo-bulk-cancel`, `POST /b2f/v1/po-complete`, `POST /dinoco-stock/v1/dip-stock/approve` (first batch with 3 bulk-array endpoints ‚Äî canonical sort pattern in `docs/patterns/IDEMPOTENCY-KEY.md` ¬ßBulk endpoint considerations)
  - **Round 28** (5): `POST /b2b/v1/admin-stock-unlock`, `POST /b2b/v1/admin-stock-mark-oos`, `POST /b2b/v1/admin-submit-tracking`, `POST /b2f/v1/approve-reschedule`, `POST /b2f/v1/reject-resolve` (2nd bulk-array endpoint admin-submit-tracking entries[] sort by ticket_id + bulk-of-targets pattern admin-stock-unlock notify_tickets[])

## REST API Endpoints (MCP Bridge)

All under `/wp-json/dinoco-mcp/v1/` (32 endpoints, V.2.0). **Idempotency-Key wrapper**: 13/17 POST endpoints integrated (~76% MCP namespace coverage as of Round 35) ‚Äî see [`docs/audit/IDEMPOTENCY-COVERAGE.md` ¬ß MCP Cluster Coverage](docs/audit/IDEMPOTENCY-COVERAGE.md). Remaining 4 POST routes are read-only queries (product-lookup/dealer-lookup/warranty-check/kb-search) ‚Äî naturally idempotent.
- **Core**: `product-lookup` (+stock_status), `dealer-lookup`, `warranty-check`, `kb-search`, `kb-export`, `catalog-full`, `distributor-notify`, `distributor-list`, `kb-suggest`, `brand-voice-submit`
- **Claims**: `claim-manual-create`, `claim-manual-update`, `claim-manual-status`, `claim-manual-list`, `claim-status`
- **Leads (P1)**: `lead-create`, `lead-update`, `lead-list`, `lead-get/{id}`, `lead-followup-schedule`
- **Phase 2**: `warranty-registered`, `member-motorcycle`, `member-assets`, `customer-link`, `dealer-sla-report`, `distributor-get/{id}`, `product-compatibility`
- **Phase 3**: `kb-updated`, `inventory-changed`, `moto-catalog`, `dashboard-inject-metrics`, `lead-attribution`

## REST API Endpoints (GDPR)

All under `/wp-json/dinoco-gdpr/v1/` (V.1.0 stubs, flag `dinoco_gdpr_enabled` default=0 ‚Üí returns 503):
- `POST /my-data-export` ‚Äî logged-in user requests data export (queue + admin review)
- `POST /my-data-delete` ‚Äî logged-in user requests account deletion (queue + anonymize/hard-delete decision)
- `GET /my-data-status` ‚Äî check status of active request

Schema `wp_dinoco_gdpr_requests` (id, user_id, type, status, created_at, processed_at, notes) lazy-install via `dbDelta` on first activation. Data scope: wp_users + wp_usermeta + distributor CPT + warranties + claims + B2B orders + LINE messages (via agent:3000). Full implementation + admin review UI deferred to Phase 6.

## Required WordPress Constants

- `DINOCO_LINE_CHANNEL_ID` ‚Äî LINE OAuth app ID
- `DINOCO_LINE_CHANNEL_SECRET` ‚Äî LINE OAuth channel secret (required for ID Token verify)
- `DINOCO_LINE_REDIRECT_URI` ‚Äî OAuth callback URL
- `B2B_LINE_ACCESS_TOKEN` ‚Äî Bot token for LINE notifications
- `B2B_ADMIN_GROUP_ID` ‚Äî Admin LINE group for alerts
- `DINOCO_GITHUB_TOKEN` ‚Äî GitHub PAT for sync engine
- `DINOCO_GITHUB_REPO` ‚Äî GitHub repo (e.g., `Vrprammz/DINOCO-SYSTEM-Front-End---Back-End`)
- `DINOCO_GITHUB_WEBHOOK_SECRET` ‚Äî Webhook signature secret
- `B2F_LIFF_ID` ‚Äî ýπÉý∏äýπâý∏ïý∏±ý∏ßýπÄý∏îý∏µý∏¢ý∏ßý∏Åý∏±ý∏ö `B2B_LIFF_ID` (auto-fallback ýπÑý∏°ýπàý∏ïýπâý∏≠ý∏áý∏ïý∏±ýπâý∏áýπÅý∏¢ý∏Å)
- `LIFF_AI_SECRET_KEY` ‚Äî LIFF AI auth HMAC key (required)
- `LIFF_AI_JWT_SECRET` ‚Äî LIFF AI JWT signing key (auto-generated to wp_option if undefined)
- `LIFF_AI_AGENT_URL` ‚Äî OpenClaw agent proxy URL (default `http://agent:3000`)
- `LIFF_AI_AGENT_KEY` ‚Äî agent proxy bearer token
- `DINOCO_JWT` ‚Äî HMAC secret for God Mode margin-analysis JWT (V.42.17)
- `B2F_DISABLED` ‚Äî kill switch for B2F module (optional boolean)
- `B2B_WALKIN_BANK_*` ‚Äî optional walk-in bank override (BANK_NAME, BANK_NAME_EN, BANK_ACCOUNT, BANK_HOLDER, BANK_CODE, BANK_LOGO_URL, PROMPTPAY_ID) ‚Äî falls back to `B2B_BANK_*` if undefined
- `DINOCO_SENTRY_DSN` ‚Äî optional Sentry DSN for Observability snippet (V.1.0). Requires `composer require sentry/sentry` + `dinoco_obs_sentry_enabled=1` to activate
- `DINOCO_SENTRY_ENV` ‚Äî optional Sentry environment tag (default `production`)
- `DINOCO_SENTRY_SAMPLE_RATE` ‚Äî optional transaction sample rate 0.0-1.0 (default 0.1)

## File Organization

Files are named by feature area with bracket prefixes:
- `[System] *` ‚Äî Member-facing features (dashboard, registration, claims, profile)
- `[Admin System] *` ‚Äî Admin/management features (analytics, CRM, AI, knowledge base)
- `[B2B] Snippet N: *` ‚Äî B2B distributor modules (versioned snippets)
- `[B2F] Snippet N: *` ‚Äî B2F factory purchasing modules (Snippets 0-11)
- `[GitHub] *` ‚Äî Webhook integration

Each file is a self-contained module with its own version number (e.g., V.32.x, V.34.x).

### DB_ID Header (V.32.0)

Every snippet file includes a `DB_ID: NNN` header in its comment block (first 1000 chars). This integer maps to the `id` column in the `wp_snippets` table. The GitHub Webhook Sync engine (`dinoco_extract_db_id()`) uses DB_ID as the **primary** matching key when syncing code from GitHub to WordPress. If a file has no DB_ID header, it falls back to normalized filename matching.

## Development Notes

- **Phase 1 Audit Remediation** (V.32.6/V.7.6/V.1.7/V.11.4/V.7.4/V.3.8, 2026-04-17 ‚Äî audit `AUDIT-REPORT-2026-04-17.md`): shipped 12 low-risk ship-blockers in 5 batched commits. **Security**: removed unsecured `/webhook/telegram` plaintext fallback (S4 ‚Äî secret-path is now the sole auth gate) + `npm audit fix` across 3 roots closes path-to-regexp ReDoS + vite 3-CVE bundle (0 vulnerabilities across all lockfiles now). **Correctness**: BO rate-limit on `place-order` restored (`!b2b_rate_limit()` ‚Üí `is_wp_error($rl)` per Snippet 1 V.33.7 contract ‚Äî hour+day caps were silently disabled since V.1.6 flag enablement), `b2f_format_po_detail()` PII gate defense-in-depth restored (removed self-reverting `$is_admin_gate=true` fallback ‚Äî admin LIFF without WP user now sees PII stripped until Phase 2 auth fix), enumeration flags bit-field now OR-combines (cancel_abuse=2 + qty_cap_hit=4 no longer overwrite each other), duplicate `rest_prepare_post` filter removed (superseded by `rest_prepare_b2b_order`), `user_agent` VARCHAR length aligned to schema (128 vs 255 substr ‚Äî STRICT-mode safe). **Performance**: `DINOCO_Catalog::get_by_sku()` static per-request memo (50-150ms saved per endpoint iterating items), 3 BO admin shortcodes added to `$cacheable_modules` (200-500ms saved per BO tab switch), `fetchBoBadge` polling gated by `document.visibilityState` (~50% background polling reduction when admin has multiple tabs). **UX**: amber mode badge text contrast darkened #d97706‚Üí#b45309 (5.9:1 WCAG AA vs 4.3:1 fail) across B2F Snippet 5 + 8. **Cleanup**: orphan flag `b2f_flag_ungroup_auto_hide` already removed in upstream commit 9e70b4c (declared but never consumed ‚Äî auto-hide driven by `admin_display_mode` column from Phase 4 migration). **Deferred to Phase 2** (require design/auth work): S1/S2/S3 auth hardening (LIFF AI + B2F HMAC + OpenClaw unauth POSTs), BO stock double-subtract chain (BUG-C2/C3/C5/C6/C7), LINE postback dispatcher gap (BUG-C5), `update_meta_cache` priming on `/order-history` + `/bo-queue`, Phase 4 migration live run. Files touched: `[B2B] Snippet 16 V.1.7`, `[B2F] Snippet 2 V.11.4`, `[B2B] Snippet 15 V.7.6`, `[Admin System] DINOCO Admin Dashboard V.32.6`, `[B2F] Snippet 5 V.7.4`, `[B2F] Snippet 8 V.7.4`, `openclawminicrm/proxy/index.js`, 3 package-lock.json.
- **Deployment**: Files are WordPress code snippets deployed via GitHub Webhook Sync (V.34.1). Push to `main` ‚Üí webhook auto-syncs all snippets using DB_ID matching. Manual sync available via dashboard.
- **Debt System**: Atomic MySQL transactions (`b2b_debt_add/subtract` in Snippet 13) with `FOR UPDATE` lock. `b2b_recalculate_debt()` is single-SQL source of truth. All debt mutations go through Snippet 13 ‚Äî direct `update_field('current_debt')` is blocked.
- **Timezone**: Hardcoded to `Asia/Bangkok` throughout.
- **Language**: UI text and code comments are primarily in Thai.
- **Security patterns**: WordPress nonce verification, honeypot fields, rate limiting via transients, `sanitize_text_field`/`esc_html`/`esc_url` for output.
- **CSS scoping**: Styles are inline within each PHP file. Recent work has focused on scoping CSS to avoid cross-module conflicts.
- **Inventory System** (V.6.0): `dinoco_stock_add/subtract()` ýπÉý∏ô Snippet 15 ‚Äî atomic `FOR UPDATE` lock per SKU + warehouse sync. ý∏ïý∏±ý∏îý∏™ý∏ïýπáý∏≠ý∏Åý∏ïý∏≠ý∏ô `awaiting_confirm` (ýπÑý∏°ýπàýπÉý∏äýπà shipped) ý∏úýπàý∏≤ý∏ô hook `b2b_order_status_changed` priority 5. Auto-cancel 30 ý∏ôý∏≤ý∏óý∏µý∏ñýπâý∏≤ý∏ïý∏±ý∏ßýπÅý∏óý∏ôýπÑý∏°ýπà confirm (`dinoco_inv_auto_cancel` cron + lazy check). `dinoco_stock_auto_status()` compute `stock_display` = in_stock/low_stock/out_of_stock (low_stock ýπÄý∏õýπáý∏ô computed ýπÑý∏°ýπàýπÄý∏Åýπáý∏ö DB) + **cascade update ancestor ý∏óý∏∏ý∏Åý∏£ý∏∞ý∏îý∏±ý∏ö** (grandchild‚Üíchild‚Üíparent). Flag `dinoco_inv_initialized` ý∏ïýπâý∏≠ý∏á true ý∏Åýπàý∏≠ý∏ô auto_status ý∏óý∏≥ý∏áý∏≤ý∏ô (Admin ý∏óý∏≥ Dip Stock ý∏Ñý∏£ý∏±ýπâý∏áýπÅý∏£ý∏Å). **3-Level SKU Hierarchy** (V.6.0): ý∏£ý∏≠ý∏áý∏£ý∏±ý∏öýπÅý∏°ýπà‚Üíý∏•ý∏πý∏Å‚Üíý∏äý∏¥ýπâý∏ôý∏™ýπàý∏ßý∏ôý∏¢ýπàý∏≠ý∏¢ (max depth 3). ý∏ïý∏±ý∏îý∏™ý∏ïýπáý∏≠ý∏ÅýπÄý∏âý∏ûý∏≤ý∏∞ leaf nodes ýπÄý∏óýπàý∏≤ý∏ôý∏±ýπâý∏ô (DD-2). Parent stock = MIN(children computed stock) recursive. B2F receive ‚Üí `dinoco_stock_add()`. Cancel ‚Üí `dinoco_stock_add()` ý∏Ñý∏∑ý∏ô leaf.

  - **Philosophy shift**: "realtime stock check on order" ‚Üí "opaque accept + admin split review" ‚Äî block **stock enumeration attack** (log‚ÇÇ(stock) probe) + enable partial fulfill workflow + eliminate `b2b_check_order_oos()` drift.

  - **14 REST endpoints** `/b2b/v1/bo-*`:

    - **Admin read**: `bo-queue` (filter status/sku/age + summary), `bo-pending-review` (server-side meta_query ‚Äî ýπÅý∏Åýπâ WP REST quirk), `bo-order-detail` (single record + fresh_snapshot real-time recompute), `bo-summary` (badge counts), `bo-restock-scan` (manual trigger)

  - **Place-order gate** (Snippet 16 hook `rest_pre_dispatch` priority 5): hard caps (qty ‚â§500/item + items ‚â§50/order) + rate limits (10/hr + 50/day via `b2b_rate_limit()` V.33.7 atomic GET_LOCK + daily qty 2000/SKU + tier value cap standard 50k ‚Üí diamond unlimited + **unique-SKU/day 20** + **suspicious qty flagger** 100/500/1000/2000 ‚Üí Telegram alert) + **artificial jitter 50-150ms** (timing side-channel defense H3).
  - **Opaque accept flow** (Snippet 2 V.34.4 C2 FIX + Snippet 3 V.41.4 C1 FIX):
    1. Customer `place-order` ‚Üí Snippet 3 fires `do_action('b2b_place_order_post_process', $order_id, $dist_id, $items, $total)` (C1)
    2. Customer `confirm_order` postback ‚Üí Snippet 2 checks `b2b_bo_flag_enabled($dist_id)` BEFORE OOS check (C2): ý∏ñýπâý∏≤ ON ‚Üí transition `draft ‚Üí pending_stock_review` + `_b2b_stock_snapshot` meta (admin-only) + `_b2b_opaque_accept_at` timestamp + increment daily counters + `b2b_log_attempt('place_order', accepted)` + notify admin Flex bucket + reply customer opaque "ý∏£ý∏≠ýπÅý∏≠ý∏îý∏°ý∏¥ý∏ôý∏ïý∏£ý∏ßý∏àý∏™ý∏≠ý∏ö 2-4 ý∏äý∏°." ‚Äî **ýπÑý∏°ýπàýπÄý∏úý∏¢ stock info**
    3. Admin receive Flex stock review bucket (no exact qty) ‚Üí ý∏Åý∏î **ý∏¢ý∏∑ý∏ôý∏¢ý∏±ý∏ôýπÄý∏ïýπáý∏°** (bo-confirm-full ‚Üí awaiting_confirm + debt full) / **Split BO** (deep-link Admin Dashboard ‚Üí Backorders tab ‚Üí modal + validate invariant `qty_fulfill + qty_bo = qty` + per-SKU compound debt + bo_queue insert) / **ý∏õý∏èý∏¥ýπÄý∏™ý∏ò** (cancelled + revert counters)
    4. Customer ýπÑý∏îýπâý∏£ý∏±ý∏ö combined Flex "‚úÖ ý∏àý∏±ý∏îý∏™ýπàý∏áý∏óý∏±ý∏ôý∏óý∏µ N ý∏äý∏¥ýπâý∏ô + ‚è≥ ý∏£ý∏≠ý∏™ý∏ïýπáý∏≠ý∏Å M ý∏äý∏¥ýπâý∏ô + ETA + [ý∏¢ý∏∑ý∏ôý∏¢ý∏±ý∏ôý∏öý∏¥ý∏•] [ý∏îý∏πý∏≠ý∏≠ýπÄý∏îý∏≠ý∏£ýπå]" (M6 FIX)
    5. Restock cron (15min) ‚Üí scan bo_queue pending + check available ‚Üí mark ready + Telegram alert
    6. Admin `bo-fulfill` ‚Üí stock subtract + debt add + FSM transition + fire `b2b_bo_items_fulfilled` action ‚Üí H5 Flash secondary order + H6 print queue + notify customer BO ready Flex (M7 FIX with [ý∏¢ý∏∑ý∏ôý∏¢ý∏±ý∏ôý∏öý∏¥ý∏• BO] [ý∏îý∏πý∏≠ý∏≠ýπÄý∏îý∏≠ý∏£ýπå] footer)
  - **Security hardening** (4 CRIT + 5 HIGH + 3 MED ý∏àý∏≤ý∏Å security-pentester review):
    - **C1 Admin Flex bucket indicator**: ýπÅý∏™ý∏îý∏á `‚úì ý∏ûý∏≠` / `‚öÝÔ∏è ý∏´ý∏°ý∏î` / `‚öÝÔ∏è ýπÑý∏°ýπàý∏ûý∏≠` ýπÑý∏°ýπàýπÄý∏úý∏¢ exact qty ýπÉý∏ô LINE group (insider threat) ‚Äî Admin Dashboard UI ýπÅý∏™ý∏îý∏á exact qty ýπÑý∏îýπâ (gated manage_options)
    - **C2 rate limit race**: `b2b_rate_limit()` V.33.7 atomic via MySQL `GET_LOCK/RELEASE_LOCK` 2s timeout + try/finally ‚Äî wrap critical section serialize across PHP workers
    - **C3 meta filter hardening**: `register_post_meta` ý∏óý∏±ýπâý∏á 8 admin-only meta keys (`_b2b_stock_snapshot`, `_b2b_enumeration_flags`, `_b2b_opaque_accept_at`, etc.) with `show_in_rest=false` + `auth_callback=manage_options` + `rest_prepare_b2b_order` filter strip meta ý∏àý∏≤ý∏Å non-admin response (defense-in-depth)
    - **C4 XSS audit log**: Security Log viewer `esc_html()` ý∏óý∏∏ý∏Å user input (IP, UA) + UA truncated 50 chars
    - **H1 CSRF**: WP admin X-WP-Nonce (wp_rest) + admin LINE LIFF JWT session token + GET read-only skip nonce
    - **H2 unique-SKU/day cap 20** + suspicious qty flagger ‚Äî block cross-SKU enumeration (Vector D)
    - **H3 artificial jitter 50-150ms** ‚Äî mask timing variance (œÉ <100ms realistic ýπÉý∏ô WP)
    - **H4 cancel grace period** (Snippet 3 V.41.3): first 5 min after order = unlimited (legitimate UX) + after grace = 2/hr + 10/day + log attempts for enumeration scan
    - **H5 undo 1 max per order** ‚Äî prevent oscillation attack (stock probe via split ‚Üí undo ‚Üí split loop)
  - **DB schema hardening** (2 CRIT + 5 HIGH ý∏àý∏≤ý∏Å database-expert review): dbDelta pattern correct (KEY syntax + $charset + PRIMARY KEY inside) + VARCHAR ýπÑý∏°ýπàýπÉý∏äýπà ENUM (ALTER-friendly) + idx_created + idx_dist_action_time + idx_status_resolved + user_agent VARCHAR(128) + DECIMAL(14,2) + sku utf8mb4_bin + FOR UPDATE lock ýπÉý∏ô bo-fulfill + chunked cleanup cron (1000/iter + 50ms gap).
  - **FSM V.1.6** (Snippet 14): 2 new states `pending_stock_review` + `partial_fulfilled` + 8 new transitions:
    - `draft ‚Üí pending_stock_review` (customer, via confirm_order BO gate)
    - `pending_stock_review ‚Üí awaiting_confirm` (admin, bo-confirm-full)
    - `pending_stock_review ‚Üí partial_fulfilled` (admin, bo-split)
    - `pending_stock_review ‚Üí cancelled` (admin/customer/system ‚Äî reject/cancel-request/timeout cron)
    - `partial_fulfilled ‚Üí awaiting_confirm` (any ‚Äî all BO resolved = fulfilled + cancelled)
    - `partial_fulfilled ‚Üí pending_stock_review` (admin, bo-undo-split 10min + 1 max)
    - `partial_fulfilled ‚Üí cancelled` (admin, manual escalation)
    - Legacy `checking_stock` ý∏¢ý∏±ý∏áý∏Ñý∏áý∏óý∏≥ý∏áý∏≤ý∏ô ‚Äî backward compat ý∏™ý∏≥ý∏´ý∏£ý∏±ý∏ö orders ýπÄý∏Åýπàý∏≤ýπÅý∏•ý∏∞ flag OFF path
  - **6 cron jobs**: `b2b_bo_restock_scan_cron` (15min ‚Äî promote pending ‚Üí ready ý∏ñýπâý∏≤ available ‚â• qty_bo) + `b2b_bo_eta_warn_cron` (daily 09:00 ‚Äî ETA < +3d alert) + `b2b_bo_pending_review_expire_cron` (hourly ‚Äî 72h auto-cancel) + `b2b_bo_enumeration_scan_cron` (hourly ‚Äî >5 cancels/24h OR >3 qty_cap_hits/24h ‚Üí Telegram `enumeration_attempt` + update `_b2b_enumeration_flags` bit field) + `b2b_bo_attempt_log_cleanup_cron` (daily 03:00 ‚Äî chunked 1000/iter + 50ms gap + 20 max iterations).

- **B2B OOS Gate Hotfix V.33.5 + V.7.4** (Phase 0 Ticket #6266, 2026-04-16): Bug ‚Äî ý∏•ý∏πý∏Åý∏Ñýπâý∏≤ý∏™ý∏±ýπàý∏á SET `DNCSETNX500IRNB` (stock=10 ý∏àý∏£ý∏¥ý∏á), ý∏£ý∏∞ý∏öý∏öý∏ïý∏≠ý∏ö "ý∏™ý∏¥ý∏ôý∏Ñýπâý∏≤ý∏´ý∏°ý∏îý∏äý∏±ýπàý∏ßý∏Ñý∏£ý∏≤ý∏ß" BO ý∏Çýπâý∏≤ý∏° admin check. Backend: `dinoco_get_wac_for_skus($skus)` batch helper ýπÉý∏ô Snippet 15 V.7.2 ‚Äî 1 SQL query ýπÄý∏îý∏µý∏¢ý∏ß + per-SKU transient cache 1 ý∏äý∏° + invalidation hook `b2f_receive_completed`. Frontend: `fetchMarginAnalysis(sku)` ý∏ïý∏≠ý∏ô `openEditCatalogModal` ý∏ñýπâý∏≤ god mode ‚Üí prefetch `window._marginContext = { total_cost, retail, ... }` ‚Üí `updateTierPreview` extend ý∏îýπâý∏ßý∏¢ profit line (`+Yý∏ø (+Z%)` ý∏™ý∏µýπÄý∏Çý∏µý∏¢ý∏ß/ýπÅý∏îý∏á) client-side math ýπÑý∏°ýπàýπÄý∏£ý∏µý∏¢ý∏Å API ý∏ãýπâý∏≥ + header banner ýπÅý∏™ý∏îý∏áý∏ïýπâý∏ôý∏óý∏∏ý∏ô WAC + warning ý∏ñýπâý∏≤ incomplete (`is_incomplete=true` + `missing_wac_leaves[]`). God mode client-side class ý∏¢ý∏±ý∏áýπÉý∏äýπâý∏≠ý∏¢ý∏πýπàý∏™ý∏≥ý∏´ý∏£ý∏±ý∏ö UI gate (ý∏õý∏∏ýπàý∏° delete/edit) ýπÅý∏ïýπà cost data ý∏ñý∏πý∏Å enforce ý∏óý∏µýπà backend ‚Äî DevTools manipulation ýπÄý∏Çýπâý∏≤ýπÑý∏°ýπàý∏ñý∏∂ý∏á
  - **V.42.16 Sum Integrity Check (Phase 2 Redesign)**: ýπÄý∏õý∏•ý∏µýπàý∏¢ý∏ô concept ý∏àý∏≤ý∏Å "ýπÅý∏ôý∏∞ý∏ôý∏≥ý∏£ý∏≤ý∏Ñý∏≤" ‚Üí "ý∏ïý∏£ý∏ßý∏àý∏Ñý∏ßý∏≤ý∏°ý∏Ñý∏£ý∏öý∏Çý∏≠ý∏áý∏£ý∏≤ý∏Ñý∏≤ SET":
    - **Header card**: parent / sum(children effective) / margin ý∏ûý∏£ýπâý∏≠ý∏° status
      * `ok` (|diff| < 1%) ‚Äî ýπÄý∏Çý∏µý∏¢ý∏ß "ý∏£ý∏≤ý∏Ñý∏≤ý∏™ý∏°ý∏îý∏∏ý∏•"
      * `loss` (sum > parent) ‚Äî ýπÅý∏îý∏á "ýπÅý∏°ýπàý∏ñý∏πý∏Åý∏Åý∏ßýπàý∏≤ý∏úý∏•ý∏£ý∏ßý∏°ý∏•ý∏πý∏Å" (ý∏Çý∏≤ý∏¢ýπÅý∏°ýπàýπÅý∏•ýπâý∏ßý∏Çý∏≤ý∏îý∏óý∏∏ý∏ô)
      * `profit` (sum < parent) ‚Äî ý∏üýπâý∏≤ "ýπÅý∏°ýπàýπÅý∏ûý∏áý∏Åý∏ßýπàý∏≤ý∏úý∏•ý∏£ý∏ßý∏°ý∏•ý∏πý∏Å" (ý∏°ý∏≤ý∏£ýπåý∏àý∏¥ýπâý∏ôý∏öý∏ßý∏Å)
    - **Effective cost**: ý∏ñýπâý∏≤ child ýπÄý∏õýπáý∏ô sub-SET ýπÉý∏äýπâ `sum(grandchildren prices)` ýπÅý∏óý∏ô child.price (ý∏£ý∏≤ý∏Ñý∏≤ý∏àý∏£ý∏¥ý∏á ýπÑý∏°ýπàýπÉý∏äýπà sub-SET stale)
    - **Per-child badge**: `ý∏£ý∏≤ý∏Ñý∏≤ý∏àý∏£ý∏¥ý∏á Xý∏ø ¬∑ Y% ý∏Çý∏≠ý∏áýπÅý∏°ýπà` (contribution % ýπÑý∏°ýπàýπÉý∏äýπà suggestion)
    - **Sub-SET integrity**: ý∏ñýπâý∏≤ child ý∏°ý∏µ grandchildren ‚Üí ýπÄý∏óý∏µý∏¢ý∏ö `sum(gc)` ý∏Åý∏±ý∏ö `child.price` ‚Üí ýπÅý∏™ý∏îý∏á warning ý∏ñýπâý∏≤ý∏ïýπàý∏≤ý∏á `|diff| >= 1%` (e.g. "ý∏•ý∏πý∏Åý∏£ý∏ßý∏°ýπÄý∏Åý∏¥ý∏ô +2,250ý∏ø (+41%)")
    - **Per-grandchild badge**: `ý∏£ý∏≤ý∏Ñý∏≤ý∏àý∏£ý∏¥ý∏á ¬∑ Y% ý∏Çý∏≠ý∏á sub-SET/ýπÅý∏°ýπà` (contribution %)
    - Helper `_priceOf(sku)` ‚Äî case-insensitive price lookup ý∏úýπàý∏≤ý∏ô `cat()`
    - Live update ýπÄý∏´ý∏°ý∏∑ý∏≠ý∏ô V.42.15 (debounced 250ms)
    - Removed: equal-split "ýπÅý∏ôý∏∞ý∏ôý∏≥ Xý∏ø" + diff% badges (concept ý∏úý∏¥ý∏î)

- **Product Data Consolidation** (V.35.0): ý∏£ý∏≤ý∏Ñý∏≤ tier/ý∏™ýπàý∏ßý∏ôý∏•ý∏î/category/MOQ/boxes_per_unit ý∏¢ýπâý∏≤ý∏¢ý∏°ý∏≤ý∏àý∏±ý∏îý∏Åý∏≤ý∏£ý∏óý∏µýπà Product Catalog (Inventory DB) ýπÄý∏ûý∏µý∏¢ý∏áý∏óý∏µýπàýπÄý∏îý∏µý∏¢ý∏ß. - **setTimeout gotcha**: Admin Dashboard overrides `window.setTimeout` to capture timers >= 3s for auto-refresh control. Toast/notification auto-dismiss must use `(window._dncAutoRefresh && window._dncAutoRefresh.origSetTimeout) || setTimeout` to bypass the override.
- **Modal pattern**: Modals use event delegation for dynamically created elements. Backdrop click-to-close is a common interaction pattern.
- **View/Edit toggle pattern**: Profile page uses Facebook-style view-mode cards. Info is read-only by default; tap "ýπÅý∏ÅýπâýπÑý∏Ç" to expand the form. Save button only appears when a section is in edit mode.
- **Product Data Source of Truth** (V.32.6): Custom table `wp_dinoco_products` (Snippet 15) is the single source of truth for ALL product fields: pricing (base_price = retail, price_silver/gold/platinum/diamond = **% discount** per tier), stock_status, oos_timestamp, oos_duration_hours, oos_eta_date, b2b_discount_percent (Standard tier default), boxes_per_unit, units_per_box, min_order_qty, category, compatible_models, b2b_visible. Central helper `b2b_get_product_data($sku)` (Snippet 1) reads from custom table with ACF fallback. Batch helper `b2b_get_product_data_batch()` returns all products in 1 query. All WRITE operations must dual-write: custom table + ACF (for backward compat). All READ operations should use custom table helpers first, fallback ACF. `b2b_get_sku_data_map()` (Snippet 3) now batch-reads from custom table including pricing tiers.
- **Box Calculation** (V.32.9): `boxes_per_unit` = ý∏™ý∏¥ý∏ôý∏Ñýπâý∏≤ 1 ý∏äý∏¥ýπâý∏ôýπÉý∏äýπâý∏Åý∏µýπàý∏Åý∏•ýπàý∏≠ý∏á (ý∏Çý∏≠ý∏áýπÉý∏´ý∏çýπà, default 1). `units_per_box` = 1 ý∏Åý∏•ýπàý∏≠ý∏áýπÉý∏™ýπàý∏™ý∏¥ý∏ôý∏Ñýπâý∏≤ýπÑý∏îýπâý∏Åý∏µýπàý∏äý∏¥ýπâý∏ô (ý∏Çý∏≠ý∏áýπÄý∏•ýπáý∏ÅýπÅý∏ûýπáý∏Ñý∏£ý∏ßý∏°, default 1). Mutual exclusive: ý∏´ýπâý∏≤ý∏°ý∏ïý∏±ýπâý∏áý∏óý∏±ýπâý∏áý∏Ñý∏πýπà > 1. ý∏™ý∏πý∏ïý∏£: `units_per_box > 1 ‚Üí ceil(qty / upb)`, `boxes_per_unit > 1 ‚Üí qty * bpu`, ý∏óý∏±ýπâý∏áý∏Ñý∏πýπà = 1 ‚Üí qty. Helpers: `b2b_get_units_per_box()`, `b2b_compute_boxes_for_qty()` (Snippet 1). ýπÉý∏äýπâýπÉý∏ô `b2b_calculate_total_boxes()` + `b2b_calculate_box_manifest()` ý∏™ý∏≥ý∏´ý∏£ý∏±ý∏ö Flash shipping PNO count.

- **B2F V.7.0 Order Intent System** (2026-04-17 deployed ‚Äî flags OFF default): Admin LIFF B2F E-Catalog rework. Admin ý∏™ý∏±ýπàý∏áý∏Çý∏≠ý∏áý∏àý∏≤ý∏ÅýπÇý∏£ý∏áý∏áý∏≤ý∏ôýπÑý∏îýπâ 3 ý∏£ý∏∞ý∏îý∏±ý∏ö ý∏äý∏±ý∏îýπÄý∏àý∏ô:
  - **üü£ ý∏äý∏∏ý∏îýπÄý∏ïýπáý∏°** (`full_set` / `production_mode=set_assembled`) ‚Äî ý∏™ý∏±ýπàý∏áý∏äý∏∏ý∏îýπÄý∏ïýπáý∏° ýπÄý∏äýπàý∏ô ý∏Åý∏±ý∏ôý∏•ýπâý∏° crash bar SET
  - **üüÝ ýπÅý∏¢ý∏Åý∏äý∏∏ý∏î** (`sub_unit` / `production_mode=sub_unit`) ‚Äî ý∏™ý∏±ýπàý∏áý∏äý∏∏ý∏îý∏¢ýπàý∏≠ý∏¢ L+R pair (Pannier Rack, ý∏äý∏∏ý∏îý∏öý∏ô/ý∏•ýπàý∏≤ý∏á)
  - **‚ö™ ý∏äý∏¥ýπâý∏ôýπÄý∏îý∏µýπàý∏¢ý∏ß** (`single_leaf` / `production_mode=single`) ‚Äî ý∏™ý∏±ýπàý∏á 1 ý∏äý∏¥ýπâý∏ô ýπÄý∏äýπàý∏ô Top Rack ýπÄý∏îý∏µýπàý∏¢ý∏ß
  - **üüÝ DINOCO ý∏õý∏£ý∏∞ý∏Åý∏≠ý∏ö** (`cross_factory_assembly`, hidden default) ‚Äî SET ý∏óý∏µýπà DINOCO ý∏£ý∏ßý∏° parts ý∏àý∏≤ý∏Åý∏´ý∏•ý∏≤ý∏¢ýπÇý∏£ý∏áý∏áý∏≤ý∏ô (ýπÄý∏äýπàý∏ô box+rack ý∏àý∏≤ý∏Åý∏Ñý∏ôý∏•ý∏∞ýπÇý∏£ý∏áý∏áý∏≤ý∏ô) ‚Äî auto-hide ý∏úýπàý∏≤ý∏ô `admin_display_mode=as_parts` ýπÄý∏°ý∏∑ýπàý∏≠ `missing_leaves>0` (ý∏£ý∏∞ý∏öý∏ö stock DD-2 assemble ý∏ïý∏≠ý∏ôý∏Çý∏≠ý∏áýπÄý∏Çýπâý∏≤ý∏Ñý∏£ý∏ö admin ýπÑý∏°ýπàý∏ïýπâý∏≠ý∏áý∏àý∏±ý∏îý∏Åý∏≤ý∏£)
  - **3 axes orthogonal**: `production_mode` (physical ‚Äî 4 values) + `confirmation_status` (confirmed/auto_synced) + `admin_display_mode` (auto/as_set/as_parts ‚Äî UI override)
  - **Ungroup System 3 ways**: (1) Auto-detect migration via `missing_leaves>0` (2) Bulk action Admin Makers tab (max 200 SKUs) (3) Per-SKU manual toggle
  - **Schema V.11.0**: Junction `wp_dinoco_product_makers` +6 columns (production_mode, confirmation_status, admin_display_mode, missing_leaves_count, confirmed_by, confirmed_at) + composite indexes `idx_maker_prod_display` + `idx_maker_confirmation` + 2 CHECK constraints (MySQL 8.0.16+ enforces; PHP validator = primary defense) + observations ENUM extend `classification_change`. File: `B2F-SCHEMA-V11.sql` (root-level)
  - **2 Feature flags** (wp_options, default=false, dependency chain enforced): `b2f_flag_v11_explicit_mode` (backend returns new fields) ‚Üí `b2f_flag_order_intent` (requires v11). Previously planned 3rd flag `b2f_flag_ungroup_auto_hide` was removed in Phase 1 audit remediation (2026-04-17, BUG-H8) ‚Äî it was orphan (declared + UI-toggleable + dependency-checked but never consumed by business logic). Auto-hide is driven by `admin_display_mode='as_parts'` column set by Phase 4 migration when `missing_leaves>0`, not by a runtime flag.
  - **Error codes** (Snippet 1 V.7.0): `B2F_ERR_INVALID_ORDER_MODE` 400, `B2F_ERR_SOURCE_SKU_NOT_ANCESTOR` 400, `B2F_ERR_UNDO_WINDOW_EXPIRED` 410, `B2F_ERR_CHECK_CONSTRAINT` 422, `B2F_ERR_STALE_JUNCTION_WRITE` 409, `B2F_ERR_BULK_LIMIT_EXCEEDED` 400, `B2F_ERR_MYSQL_VERSION_TOO_LOW` warning-log, `B2F_ERR_MIGRATION_IN_PROGRESS` 503
  - **PII protection**: `poi_intent_notes` is admin-only (REST callback gate ýπÉý∏ô `b2f_format_po_detail()` strips for non-admin). Maker LIFF V.4.3 shows mode badge only (no intent_notes). PO Image omits intent_notes.
  - **Central cache hook**: `do_action('b2f_junction_updated', $maker_id)` ‚Äî 4 mutation points fire, listener invalidates `b2f_maker_products_v11_{maker_id}` + `b2f_maker_products_source_{maker_id}` transients (10min TTL)
  - **DD-3 composite merge key**: Create-PO uses `$merged["{$sku}|{$order_mode}|{$source_sku}"]` ‚Äî preserves intent per item when same SKU ordered with different modes
  - **Cart persistence**: LIFF Snippet 8 V.7.0 uses localStorage `b2f_cart_v7_{maker_id}` (schema v7 with `_schema:7` marker) ‚Äî persists across reloads
  - **Undo submit**: `POST /b2f/v1/po-undo-submit` ‚Äî 30s DB-clock window + dual auth (WP nonce OR X-B2F-Token) + FOR UPDATE + FSM draft‚Üícancelled
  - **Rollout (no canary per user decision)**: Flip 3 flags ON sequentially after migration. Rollback = `update_option(flag, false)` instant revert
  - **Glossary**: `production_mode` (per-maker-SKU ‚Äî physical production) vs `admin_display_mode` (per-maker-SKU ‚Äî UI override) vs `ui_role_override` (Inventory V.42.14, global wp_dinoco_products) vs `confirmation_status` (per-maker-SKU admin review) vs `order_mode` (per-PO-item admin intent). Precedence: `admin_display_mode > ui_role_override > auto-computed production_mode`
- **B2F V.7.0 Post-Deploy Fixes + Coverage Rule** (2026-04-17, 10+ commits `c0f05aa`‚Üí`deb70a2`): After Phase 4 migration + flag flip, discovered + fixed a series of bugs and completed the long-term hierarchy coverage design:
  - **Audit V.3.4 ‚Üí V.3.11** ‚Äî dry-run ALTER was guarded `if (!$dry_run)` but SELECT referenced V.11 columns ‚Üí silent `$wpdb->get_results` fail ‚Üí 0-row preview. Fix: ALTER always runs (idempotent INFORMATION_SCHEMA guards) + `$wpdb->last_error` check + REST top-level `message` field + frontend errors[] render in error branch. V.3.5: live migration hit `chk_confirmed_consistency` CHECK rejection when classification set `confirmation_status='confirmed'` for legacy_cpt rows without populating `confirmed_by`+`confirmed_at` ‚Üí branch UPDATE by decision status, populate both fields. V.3.6: `POST /purge-stale-prices` utility ‚Äî zero-out `unit_cost=<sentinel>` (default 666) for cleanup. V.3.7: `POST /sync-missing-intermediates` + UI card for coverage-rule cleanup. V.3.10 (review fixes): endpoint note on kill-switch flag location. V.3.11: Phase 4 migration lock auto-expire (DB-H6)
  - **Snippet 0.5 V.1.3 ‚Üí V.1.6** ‚Äî (V.1.3) bypass ACF cache: `get_post_meta()` instead of `get_field()` in `b2f_dual_write_to_junction()` ‚Äî ACF's `acf_get_value` caches per-request; save_post hook fires from `wp_update_post()` BEFORE `update_field()` ‚Üí stale 666 cached ‚Üí junction stuck. WP object cache invalidated reliably by `update_post_meta`. (V.1.4) Reactive hierarchy coverage auto-sync after every UPSERT. (V.1.5) `b2f_flag_coverage_autosync` kill-switch (default ON). (V.1.6) DB-C1 CHECK constraint fix
  - **Snippet 1 V.7.0 ‚Üí V.7.3** ‚Äî (V.7.1) Coverage Rule helpers: `b2f_get_parents_for_sku`, `b2f_is_sku_registered_for_maker`, `b2f_is_coverage_complete($sku, $maker_id, $visited, $known_set)`, `b2f_load_maker_sku_set($maker_id)`, `b2f_auto_sync_parent_coverage`, `b2f_insert_auto_sync_junction_row`, `b2f_detect_missing_intermediates`, `b2f_defer_junction_updates_state` (batched hook fire). (V.7.2/3) review fixes: pre-check before INSERT (HIGH-1), pre-loaded maker SKU set to eliminate N+1 (HIGH-2), batched `b2f_junction_updated` hook fire per walk (HIGH-3), migration-lock defer via `wp_schedule_single_event('b2f_replay_coverage_autosync', [$sku, $mid])` (MEDIUM-2), iteration cap 100 in detect loop (LOW-2)
  - **Snippet 2 V.11.0 ‚Üí V.11.4** ‚Äî (V.11.1) `maker_profile.stats.unconfirmed_count` counts SETs only (not sub_unit+single) + skip virtual products ‚Üí fixed "13 SET ý∏£ý∏≠ý∏¢ý∏∑ý∏ôý∏¢ý∏±ý∏ô" inflation to accurate 9. (V.11.2) Always call `b2f_dual_write_to_junction()` at end of save endpoint ‚Äî V.10.1 gate was OFF under shadow=ON relying on hook but hook read stale values. (V.11.3) `b2f_compute_set_costs_v918()` runs unconditionally ‚Äî SET `unit_cost` = sum(leaves.unit_cost) always (removes `$flag_junction ? $products : compute(...)` gate). Design: SET has NO manual price ‚Äî it's an aggregate. Stale junction values become dead data. (V.11.4) Phase 1 audit BUG-C1/C4/H1 fixes
  - **Snippet 5 V.7.1 ‚Üí V.7.4** ‚Äî (V.7.2) SET header gets inline price/MOQ/lead inputs (walked back to V.7.3). (V.7.3) SET price input removed in favor of read-only `.b2f-set-price-ro` badge ‚Äî green ‚úì (complete), amber ‚öÝ (partial, missing leaves in tooltip), red ‚öÝ (no leaves priced). MOQ + lead_time still editable. batchSaveProducts + updateDirtyCount extended for `.b2f-set-header[data-pid]`. (V.7.4) Phase 1 audit UX-C3 amber contrast fix
  - **Snippet 8 V.7.0 ‚Üí V.7.4** ‚Äî (V.7.1) Filter chips V.7.0 taxonomy: 3 chips ORDER_INTENT_ENABLED (üü£ ý∏äý∏∏ý∏îýπÄý∏ïýπáý∏° / üüÝ ýπÅý∏¢ý∏Åý∏äý∏∏ý∏î / ‚ö™ ý∏äý∏¥ýπâý∏ôýπÄý∏îý∏µýπàý∏¢ý∏ß) derived from `production_mode`; filter keys align `order_mode` names (`full_set`/`sub_unit`/`single_leaf`). (V.7.2) Chip counts follow model filter + transparent model cards (removed car bg/border/shadow, üöï‚ÜíüèçÔ∏è fallback). (V.7.3) `getModelImage()` 3 data-shape bugs: keyed object (not array ‚Äî `Object.values()`), `name` field (not `model_name`), `image` field (not `image_url`). Lazy `_modelImageMap` cache invalidated on `loadProducts`. SET Detail mode toggle sticky (`position:sticky; top:56px`) ‚Äî fixes toggle disappearing when scrolling into items (user had to press Back). (V.7.4) Phase 1 audit UX-C3 amber contrast fix
  - **Coverage Rule (long-term design)** ‚Äî "SKU X registered for Maker M ‚áî explicit junction row OR (X has children AND all children covered recursively)". Leaves = source of truth; intermediate + top SETs auto-derive. Implemented as 3-layer solution:
    - **Layer 1 (Reactive)** ‚Äî Snippet 0.5 V.1.5 calls `b2f_auto_sync_parent_coverage($maker_id, $sku)` after every dual-write UPSERT. Admin register leaf ‚Üí walks up hierarchy ‚Üí any ancestor with full coverage auto-INSERT into junction. Respects blacklist, migration lock (defers via cron), depth cap 10. Gated by `b2f_flag_coverage_autosync` default ON
    - **Layer 2 (Bulk cleanup)** ‚Äî Audit `POST /dinoco-b2f-audit/v1/sync-missing-intermediates` + UI card "üîó Sync Missing Intermediates (Coverage Rule)" with Dry-Run + Sync buttons. Scans all makers, returns grouped preview by maker. Rate limit 5/hr
    - **Layer 3 (Rendering)** ‚Äî Auto-added intermediates have `unit_cost=0` + `confirmation_status='auto_synced'` + `notes='auto-synced (coverage rule)'` + `legacy_cpt_id=0`. LIFF reads via `b2f_compute_set_costs_v918()` computed from leaves. Admin Makers tab renders full row (was separator label)
  - **Design decision: SET has no manual price** ‚Äî SET `unit_cost` = sum of leaves (computed on every API response). Admin edits leaves only. Prevents stale junction values (e.g. 666 from ACF-era backfill) from breaking LIFF display. Makers tab shows computed value as read-only badge with color-coded completeness status
  - **Reactive kill-switch**: `update_option('b2f_flag_coverage_autosync', '0')` ‚Üí disable auto-sync instant. Bulk endpoint still works manually
  - **Commits**: `c0f05aa` V.3.4 dry-run / `119d1f3` V.3.5 CHECK constraint / `55a0a27` V.7.1 chips / `6b2666a` V.11.1 stats / `1e24488` V.7.2 chip counts+cards / `51e70c7` V.7.3 image+toggle+purge / `2e20e71` V.7.2 SET inputs / `4b11c97` V.11.2 dual-write timing / `d8ba9e8` V.1.3 ACF bypass / `7e6b726` V.11.3+V.7.3 SET auto-compute / `9e70b4c` coverage 3-layer / `a5d44ea` review fixes / `deb70a2` V.3.11 lock auto-expire

- **Manual Invoice Picker Double-Discount Fix V.34.4 + V.34.5** (2026-04-28, 2 commits `a9c21ea` + `0110d1a`): Bug ‚Äî Multi-Picker ýπÄý∏•ý∏∑ý∏≠ý∏Å SET (catalog ý∏ø8,800 -20%) ý∏≠ý∏≠ý∏Åý∏£ý∏≤ý∏Ñý∏≤ ý∏ø5,632 (ý∏Ñý∏ßý∏£ ý∏ø7,040). Root cause: 4 call-sites (`invPickProduct` / `invPickSingleFromMulti` / `invSubmitMultiPicker` + `invApplyProductToRow` ýπÉý∏äýπâýπÉý∏ô autocomplete) ý∏™ýπàý∏á `unit_price = invGetRankPrice(p)` (= ý∏£ý∏≤ý∏Ñý∏≤ý∏îý∏µý∏•ýπÄý∏•ý∏≠ý∏£ýπå catalog √ó (1-disc%) ý∏´ý∏±ý∏ÅýπÅý∏•ýπâý∏ß) **ý∏ûý∏£ýπâý∏≠ý∏°** `discount_raw = disc%` ‚Üí `invRecalc` ý∏Ñý∏≥ý∏ôý∏ßý∏ì `effective = unit_price √ó (1 - disc%)` ý∏Ñý∏¥ý∏îý∏™ýπàý∏ßý∏ôý∏•ý∏îý∏ãýπâý∏≥ý∏äý∏±ýπâý∏ôý∏óý∏µýπàý∏™ý∏≠ý∏á.
  - **V.34.4 (`a9c21ea`)**: ýπÄý∏ûý∏¥ýπàý∏° helper `invGetRankPriceInfo(p)` ý∏Ñý∏∑ý∏ô `{base, disc, effective}`. 4 call-sites ýπÉý∏äýπâ `info.base` (catalog/retail = 8,800) ýπÄý∏õýπáý∏ô `unit_price` + `info.disc + '%'` (20%) ýπÄý∏õýπáý∏ô `discount_raw` ‚Üí recalc 8,800 √ó 0.80 = 7,040 ‚úì. Picker modal display ý∏¢ý∏±ý∏áýπÇý∏äý∏ßýπå `info.effective` (ý∏£ý∏≤ý∏Ñý∏≤ý∏îý∏µý∏•ýπÄý∏•ý∏≠ý∏£ýπå) ý∏úýπàý∏≤ý∏ô `invGetRankPrice()` wrapper.
  - **V.34.5 (`0110d1a`, post-review remediation 1 HIGH + 2 MED + 2 LOW)**:
    - **HIGH-1**: Legacy unmigrated tier price (`price_<rank> > 100` absolute, pre-V.32.6 `_dinoco_tier_pricing_migrated`) + `b2b_discount_percent=0` ‚Üí V.34.4 emit `unit_price=8,800, disc=''` ýπÅý∏™ý∏îý∏á catalog ýπÅý∏óý∏ô dealer. Fix: `invGetRankPriceInfo()` derive implicit `disc% = round((1 - effective/base) √ó 10000)/100` ýπÄý∏°ý∏∑ýπàý∏≠ `disc=0 && effective<base`. ý∏Ñý∏£ý∏≠ý∏öý∏Ñý∏•ý∏∏ý∏° `dealer_price`-only legacy products
    - **MED-2**: ý∏•ý∏ö `_invDiscRaw()` orphan dead code (logic ý∏¢ýπâý∏≤ý∏¢ýπÄý∏Çýπâý∏≤ `invGetRankPriceInfo`)
    - **MED-3**: Comment ýπÉý∏ô `invApplyProductToRow` ý∏ïý∏£ý∏áý∏Åý∏±ý∏ö code (`price` arg = last fallback when both `info.base` + `info.effective` = 0)
    - **LOW-4**: Extract `_invPickerVals(p, fallback)` helper ‚Äî unified fallback chain ýπÉý∏äýπâý∏óý∏±ýπâý∏á 3 call-sites
    - **LOW-5**: Picker chip + multi-picker grid cell `title` attr "catalog ý∏ø8,800 (-20%)" hover tooltip ý∏äýπàý∏ßý∏¢ admin ý∏¢ý∏∑ý∏ôý∏¢ý∏±ý∏ôý∏£ý∏≤ý∏Ñý∏≤ catalog vs dealer ý∏Åýπàý∏≠ý∏ôýπÄý∏•ý∏∑ý∏≠ý∏Å
  - **Trace verification** (worst case legacy): `catalog=8,800 + price_silver=7,040 (absolute) + b2b_discount_percent=0 + dealer_price=7,040` ‚Üí V.34.4 `info={base:8800, disc:0, effective:7040}` ‚Üí emit `8,800, ''` ‚Üí recalc 8,800 ‚ùå ‚Üí V.34.5 derive `disc=20` ‚Üí emit `8,800, '20%'` ‚Üí recalc 7,040 ‚úì
  - **Edge cases**: `catalog_price=0` corrupted ‚Üí `unit_price = info.effective || fallback`, `disc=''` (safe). `discPct=100` ‚Üí `effective=0`, HIGH-1 branch `effective>0` guard skips ‚Üí keeps `disc=100` correctly

- **Manual Invoice Picker Display Change V.34.6** (2026-04-28): User feedback ý∏´ý∏•ý∏±ý∏á V.34.5 ‚Äî ý∏ïý∏≤ý∏£ý∏≤ý∏á row ý∏´ý∏•ý∏±ý∏áýπÄý∏•ý∏∑ý∏≠ý∏ÅýπÅý∏™ý∏îý∏á `unit_price=8,800 + disc=20%` (ý∏ñý∏πý∏Åý∏ïýπâý∏≠ý∏á) ýπÅý∏ïýπà picker ý∏´ý∏ôýπâý∏≤ý∏Ñýπâý∏ôý∏´ý∏≤ (single + multi) ýπÅý∏™ý∏îý∏á ý∏ø7,040 (effective/dealer) ý∏ãý∏∂ýπàý∏á mismatch ý∏Åý∏±ý∏ö row ‚Üí admin ý∏áý∏áý∏ßýπàý∏≤ý∏óý∏≥ýπÑý∏° "ý∏£ý∏≤ý∏Ñý∏≤ýπÉý∏ôý∏ïý∏≤ý∏£ý∏≤ý∏áýπÑý∏°ýπàý∏ïý∏£ý∏áý∏Åý∏±ý∏öý∏óý∏µýπàýπÄý∏´ýπáý∏ôýπÉý∏ôý∏äý∏¥ý∏õ". Edge cases verified: (1) dealer_price-only legacy `{base:0, effective:7040}` ‚Üí display 7040 + no tooltip + recalc 7040 ‚úì (2) no discount `{base:8800, disc:0}` ‚Üí display 8800 + no tooltip + recalc 8800 ‚úì (3) discPct=100 ‚Üí display 8800 + tooltip "ý∏´ý∏•ý∏±ý∏áý∏™ýπàý∏ßý∏ôý∏•ý∏î ý∏ø0 (-100%)" + recalc 0 ‚úì
- **Manual Invoice Image Push Silent Failure Observability V.34.8** (2026-04-28, commit `b656dce`): User report ‚Äî "ý∏™ý∏£ýπâý∏≤ý∏áýπÉý∏öýπÅý∏àýπâý∏áý∏´ý∏ôý∏µýπâýπÅý∏•ýπâý∏ßýπÑý∏°ýπàý∏™ýπàý∏áý∏£ý∏πý∏õ INV ý∏•ý∏áýπÑý∏õýπÉý∏ôý∏Åý∏•ý∏∏ýπàý∏°ýπÅý∏ïýπàý∏™ýπàý∏á Flex". - **Manual Invoice + Image Generator Code-Reviewer Remediation V.34.10 + V.30.8** (2026-04-28, commit `25d6f5e`): Post-V.34.9 + V.30.7 review ý∏ûý∏ö 1 HIGH + 3 MED + 4 LOW. ýπÅý∏Åýπâý∏óý∏±ýπâý∏áý∏´ý∏°ý∏î (LOW-3 + LOW-4 reviewer-verified safe, no action).
  - **HIGH-1 (V.34.10)**: V.34.9 `_invHandleAuthError` ý∏îý∏±ý∏Å 403 ý∏óý∏∏ý∏Åý∏ïý∏±ý∏ß ‚Üí non-nonce 403 (e.g. `b2b_rate_limit()` 403, BO tier mismatch, per-endpoint capability fail) ý∏Åýπá redirect ýπÑý∏õ wp-login ‚Üí admin force-logout ý∏óý∏±ýπâý∏áý∏óý∏µýπà session ý∏¢ý∏±ý∏áý∏îý∏µ + ýπÄý∏™ý∏µý∏¢ unsaved draft.   - **MED-2 (V.34.10)**: resend-line callers ýπÅý∏™ý∏îý∏á generic toast ‚Üí ý∏´ý∏•ý∏±ý∏á V.34.8 server return `data.message = "ý∏™ýπàý∏á LINE ý∏•ýπâý∏°ýπÄý∏´ý∏•ý∏ß (HTTP 429)"` ýπÅý∏ïýπà frontend ý∏óý∏±ý∏öý∏îýπâý∏ßý∏¢ hardcoded "ý∏™ýπàý∏á LINE ý∏•ýπâý∏°ýπÄý∏´ý∏•ý∏ß". **Fix**: 2 callers (`invResendLineBuilder` line 4144 + `invResendLine` line 4819) ýπÉý∏äýπâ `data.message` ý∏Åýπàý∏≠ý∏ô ‚Äî admin ýπÄý∏´ýπáý∏ô HTTP code ý∏ïý∏£ý∏á ýπÜ (429 rate limit / 401 unauthorized / etc.). ýπÑý∏°ýπàý∏°ý∏µ auto-retry ‚Äî admin ý∏ïý∏±ý∏îý∏™ý∏¥ý∏ôýπÉý∏àýπÄý∏≠ý∏á

- **Manual Invoice Stale Nonce Auto-Reload V.34.9** (2026-04-28, commit `90aafe5`): User report ‚Äî "ý∏≠ý∏≠ý∏Åý∏öý∏¥ý∏•ýπÑý∏°ýπàýπÑý∏îýπâ" + console `POST /b2b/v1/invoice/update 403` + `bo-summary` polling 403 spam + UI toast "ý∏öý∏±ý∏ôý∏óý∏∂ý∏Åý∏•ýπâý∏°ýπÄý∏´ý∏•ý∏ß: Cookie check failed". One-shot guard `_invNonceReloadShown` ý∏õýπâý∏≠ý∏áý∏Åý∏±ý∏ô prompt spam ýπÄý∏°ý∏∑ýπàý∏≠ parallel calls fail ý∏ûý∏£ýπâý∏≠ý∏°ý∏Åý∏±ý∏ô (ýπÄý∏äýπàý∏ô `bo-summary` + `invoice/update` ý∏ïý∏µ 403 ý∏óý∏±ýπâý∏áý∏Ñý∏πýπà ‚Äî admin ýπÄý∏´ýπáý∏ô confirm dialog ý∏Ñý∏£ý∏±ýπâý∏áýπÄý∏îý∏µý∏¢ý∏ß).   - **401/403-capability (ýπÑý∏°ýπàýπÉý∏äýπà nonce) handler**: redirect `/wp-login.php?redirect_to=<current_url>` (logged out / capability removed)
  - **Single-handler design**: ý∏Ñý∏£ý∏≠ý∏öý∏Ñý∏•ý∏∏ý∏° 18 endpoints + bo-summary polling ýπÇý∏îý∏¢ýπÑý∏°ýπàý∏ïýπâý∏≠ý∏áýπÄý∏Çý∏µý∏¢ý∏ô retry loop ý∏ïýπàý∏≠ call. Reload restarts clean state ‚Üí nonce ýπÉý∏´ý∏°ýπà + ýπÑý∏°ýπàý∏°ý∏µ race condition ý∏Åý∏±ý∏ö in-flight requests

  - **Affected scope**: Manual Invoice ýπÄý∏óýπàý∏≤ý∏ôý∏±ýπâý∏ô (V.34.9). bo-summary polling ýπÉý∏äýπâ nonce ýπÄý∏îý∏µý∏¢ý∏ßý∏Åý∏±ý∏ô ‚Üí fix ý∏ôý∏µýπâý∏Ñý∏£ý∏≠ý∏öý∏Ñý∏•ý∏∏ý∏°ý∏îýπâý∏ßý∏¢. - **Invoice Image Generator Observability V.30.7** (2026-04-28, commit `cec04ac`): Pairs ý∏Åý∏±ý∏ö Manual Invoice V.34.8 ‚Äî `[B2B] Snippet 10: Invoice Image Generator` instrument ý∏óý∏∏ý∏Å false-return path ýπÉý∏ô `b2b_send_invoice_image()` + `b2b_generate_invoice_pages()`. ý∏Åýπàý∏≠ý∏ôý∏´ý∏ôýπâý∏≤ý∏ôý∏µýπâ Snippet 10 ý∏°ý∏µýπÅý∏Ñýπà success log `[InvImg] Pushed N pages` ‚Äî failure paths silent.
  - **`b2b_send_invoice_image`**: 3 failure paths logged ‚Äî `fail=missing_args` (group/ticket null) / `fail=no_pages` (generate returned false) / per-batch HTTP code logged + final `OK pages=N batches=M` ý∏´ý∏£ý∏∑ý∏≠ `PARTIAL/FAIL`.   - **Proactive `admin_notices` hook** (NEW): ý∏ñýπâý∏≤ GD/FreeType missing ý∏öý∏ô server ‚Üí red admin notice ýπÅý∏™ý∏îý∏áý∏óý∏±ý∏ôý∏óý∏µý∏óý∏∏ý∏Åý∏´ý∏ôýπâý∏≤ admin (gated `manage_options`) ‚Äî ýπÑý∏°ýπàý∏ïýπâý∏≠ý∏áý∏£ý∏≠ý∏≠ý∏≠ý∏Åý∏öý∏¥ý∏•ýπÅý∏£ý∏ÅýπÄý∏ûý∏∑ýπàý∏≠ discover dependency missing.   - **End-to-end traceability**: ý∏Ñý∏£ý∏±ýπâý∏áý∏´ý∏ôýπâý∏≤ "Flex ý∏™ý∏≥ýπÄý∏£ýπáý∏àýπÅý∏ïýπàý∏£ý∏πý∏õýπÑý∏°ýπàý∏°ý∏≤" silent failure ý∏àý∏∞ trace ýπÑý∏îýπâý∏Ñý∏£ý∏ö ‚Äî `[InvNotify]` (Manual Invoice 3 sites V.34.8) ‚Üí `[InvImg]` (Snippet 10 V.30.7) ‚Üí `[Font]/[GD]` (existing internal). grep command: `tail -f wp-content/debug.log | grep -E '\[InvNotify|\[InvImg|\[Font|\[GD'`
  - **No business logic change** ‚Äî pure observability + proactive alerting

- **B2F Gotchas**:

- **Manual Shipping V.44.0 ‚Äî Full Redesign + Product Picker** (2026-04-29): RPi `manual_ship.html` (V.43.2 ‚Üí V.44.0) + `dashboard.py` (V.43.1 ‚Üí V.44.0) + B2B Snippet 3 (V.42.6 ‚Üí V.42.7). Closes 3 user pain points:
  - **Bug 1: Box Templates dropdown empty** (root cause discovered ‚Äî never worked since V.43.0). dashboard.py V.43 called `/dinoco-stock/v1/box-templates` whose `$inv_perm` requires `wp_verify_nonce()`. RPi proxy sent random `api_key` as `X-WP-Nonce` ‚Üí nonce check fails 403 ‚Üí empty list cached as `[]` in `tmp/box-templates.json`. **Fix**: NEW `/b2b/v1/rpi-box-templates` endpoint (Snippet 3 V.42.7) ‚Äî read-only proxy of `dinoco_get_all_box_templates()` with `$print_perm` X-Print-Key auth. dashboard.py `_fetch_box_templates_from_wp()` switched URL + accepts `force_refresh=True` + UI ‚Üª refresh button + `?nocache=1` query param
  - **Bug 2: No product picker** ‚Äî admin had to type/scan SKU into input. **NEW**: üîç "ý∏Ñýπâý∏ôý∏´ý∏≤ý∏™ý∏¥ý∏ôý∏Ñýπâý∏≤" button opens fullscreen modal mirroring Manual Invoice picker pattern (`invFilterPicker`/`invFilterMultiPicker`): debounced 250ms search input + filter chips (ý∏óý∏±ýπâý∏áý∏´ý∏°ý∏î/ý∏äý∏∏ý∏î SET/ýπÄý∏îý∏µýπàý∏¢ý∏ß) with dynamic count badges + thumbnail rows (52√ó52, üì¶ fallback) + tap-to-pick auto-fills SKU + triggers existing `v43AutoFillFromSku()` flow. Modal: bottom-sheet on mobile, centered on desktop, ESC/backdrop close. Renders up to 100 rows (warehouse can refine via search)
  - **UX 3: Visual full redesign** ‚Äî step-by-step section flow (4 numbered cards: Sender ‚Üí Recipient ‚Üí Parcel ‚Üí Submit) with gradient step badges. Sender display 2-row (ý∏£ý∏±ý∏öý∏Çý∏≠ý∏á/ýπÉý∏öý∏õý∏∞ý∏´ý∏ôýπâý∏≤ colored tags). Touch targets ‚â• 44px throughout. Mobile-first responsive (560px breakpoint collapses grid to single column). All CSS prefixed `.dnc-ship-*` (RPi-specific scope, isolated from B2B/B2F/dinoco-admin namespaces)
  - **NEW REST endpoints** (Snippet 3 V.42.7, ~85 LOC):
    - `GET /b2b/v1/rpi-products` ‚Äî proxy of `b2b_rest_list_products()` with slim payload (sku/title/img/catalog_price/dealer_price/children/stock_status/category) + optional `?search=KW` server-side filter. X-Print-Key auth, ~500 SKU typical
    - `GET /b2b/v1/rpi-box-templates` ‚Äî proxy of `dinoco_get_all_box_templates()`. X-Print-Key auth, replaces nonce-gated `/dinoco-stock/v1/box-templates` for RPi context
  - **NEW dashboard.py routes** (V.44.0, +95 LOC):
    - `GET /api/product-search?q=KW&nocache=1` ‚Äî proxies rpi-products. tmp/products_cache.json (5min TTL) + thread-safe lock + atomic write pattern (V.43.1 M2)
    - `GET /api/box-templates?nocache=1` ‚Äî extended with cache-bypass query param + count metadata in response
  - **All V.43.2 logic preserved**: `_dimsDirty` tracking ‚Üí unset `box_template_id` if admin overrode dims after template pick. Scanner sanitize (`replace /[\r\n\t]+/`) + ASCII validate (`/^[A-Z0-9._\/-]+$/`). Template confirm-before-overwrite. Ad-hoc SKU save-back checkbox.
  - **Cache files** (in `tmp/` per systemd ReadWritePaths whitelist): `box-templates.json` (1hr TTL) + `products_cache.json` (5min TTL ‚Äî catalog edits propagate fast for picker UX)

- **B2F Maker Product Migration** (Option F Hybrid Shadow-Write, 2026-04-15/16 ‚Äî **Phase 3 ACTIVE**): ý∏¢ýπâý∏≤ý∏¢ maker product data ý∏àý∏≤ý∏Å `b2f_maker_product` CPT (drift-prone dual source of truth) ‚Üí canonical junction table `wp_dinoco_product_makers` (1:N product √ó maker). Phase 1 audit ‚Üí Phase 2 shadow-write ‚Üí Phase 3 cut-over (LIFF/Admin reads junction) ‚Üí Phase 4 CPT retirement (pending, 2-4 weeks observation).
  - **Tables (NEW ‚Äî `wp_dinoco_product_makers`)**: id, product_sku (utf8mb4_bin UPPER), maker_id, unit_cost (NATIVE currency), moq, lead_time_days, shipping_land, shipping_sea, status (active/discontinued/pending), notes, legacy_cpt_id, audit columns (created_by/updated_by/created_at/updated_at), deleted_at (soft delete). Composite unique `(product_sku, maker_id)` ‚Äî DD-3 shared leaf across makers allowed. Indexes: `idx_maker`, `idx_sku`, `idx_status`, `idx_maker_status` (hot path), `idx_legacy_cpt` (rollback), `idx_deleted`.
  - **Tables (NEW ‚Äî `wp_dinoco_maker_product_observations`)**: shadow-write drift log (observed_at, source [cpt|junction|diff], sku, maker_id, field_name, cpt_value, junction_value, diff_detected). 60-day TTL via `b2f_observations_ttl_cron` (Snippet 11 V.2.2).
  - **Schema markers** (wp_options): `b2f_schema_version='10.1'`, `b2f_schema_v10_activated` (timestamp), `b2f_phase2_backfill_state` (JSON: ran_at, cpt_migrated, orphans_added, errors, elapsed_ms, uid).
  - **Feature flags** (wp_options, default=false, whitelist enforced):
    - `b2f_flag_shadow_write` ‚Äî Phase 2 dual-write CPT ‚Üí junction (**ON** since 2026-04-16)
    - `b2f_flag_read_from_junction` ‚Äî Phase 3 reads junction-first (**ON** since 2026-04-16 ‚Äî cut-over active)
    - `b2f_flag_auto_sync_sets` ‚Äî Phase 2.5 (future, still locked)
  - **Backfill result** (Phase 2, 2026-04-16): 103 CPT rows migrated + 13 orphan SETs auto-synced = **116 junction rows total**. Orphans per maker: Happy Tech Pro (9 SETs ‚Äî DNCSETNX500002, DNCSETNX500IRNB, DNCSETNX500EX001, DNCSETNX500E002, DNCSETNX500EIRNB, DNCCBSET500X001, DNCCBSET500X002, SET0014IRON, DNCXL7500X001H) + Test Fac2 (4 SETs ‚Äî DNC4537SETGNDSTD001, DNC4537SETGNDSTD002, DNCGND37FULLSTDS, DNCGND37FULLSTDB).
  - **Phase 3 impact** (Snippet 2 V.10.0+ reads junction when `b2f_flag_read_from_junction=true`): LIFF B2F E-Catalog NX500 model filter **1 SET ‚Üí 7+ SETs** (Happy Tech Pro orphans now visible). Admin Makers tab reads junction. CPT fallback if flag off (instant rollback).
  - **REST Endpoints** (NEW namespace `/wp-json/dinoco-b2f-audit/v1/` ‚Äî 9 endpoints, registered ýπÉý∏ô `[Admin System] B2F Migration Audit` V.3.1):
    - `GET /drift` ‚Äî orphan SETs per maker (strict rule: SET ý∏°ý∏µ descendant registered ýπÅý∏ïýπà SET ýπÄý∏≠ý∏áýπÑý∏°ýπà register)
    - `GET /stale?days=90` ‚Äî stale `mp_unit_cost` (cost=0 or update > N days)
    - `GET /parity/{maker_id}` ‚Äî per-maker parity score 0-100
    - `GET /dry-run[?preview=1]` ‚Äî CSV download (columns: maker_id, maker_name, sku, issue_type, details, compatible_models, category, leaves, children, tree_view)
    - `GET /feature-flags` ‚Äî read flag state + phase info
    - `POST /activate-schema` ‚Äî dbDelta 2 canonical tables (confirm=true, rate limit 5/hr)
    - `POST /backfill` ‚Äî runs `b2f_phase2_run_backfill()` inline (Audit V.2.1 inlined ‚Äî WP Code Snippets ýπÑý∏°ýπà sync scripts/ folder). Params: `{confirm, dry_run}`. Dry-run ýπÑý∏°ýπà save state.
    - `GET /backfill-status` ‚Äî read last run summary + junction count
    - `POST /feature-flags/toggle` ‚Äî toggle whitelist flag. Guard: shadow_write ý∏ïýπâý∏≠ý∏áý∏°ý∏µ schema+backfill ý∏Åýπàý∏≠ý∏ô. Phase 3 unlocked `b2f_flag_read_from_junction`.
    - `GET /junction-snapshot` ‚Äî recent junction rows + summary (total/active/discontinued/cpt_count/diff_vs_cpt). Filter by maker_id + status.
    - `GET /observations` ‚Äî recent diff observations + summary. Filter `diff_only=1`.
  - **Key snippets**:
    - `[Admin System] B2F Migration Audit` V.3.1 ‚Äî shortcode `[b2f_migration_audit]` + 9 REST endpoints + 6 dashboard sections (parity cards, orphans, stale, Phase 2 controls 3-step, junction snapshot, diff observations) + Phase 3 flag toggle UI

  - **Gotchas**:
    - Junction table `product_sku` ý∏ïýπâý∏≠ý∏á uppercase (matches `dinoco_sku_relations` key pattern) ‚Äî SELECTs use `BINARY UPPER(sku)=UPPER(?)` via utf8mb4_bin collation
    - `legacy_cpt_id` preserved until Phase 4 (CPT retirement) ‚Äî reverse lookup ý∏™ý∏≥ý∏´ý∏£ý∏±ý∏ö rollback
    - Soft delete (`deleted_at IS NOT NULL`) preserves PO history references ‚Äî PO ý∏óý∏µýπàý∏™ý∏£ýπâý∏≤ý∏áý∏ïý∏≠ý∏ô CPT era ý∏¢ý∏±ý∏áý∏îý∏π ACF snapshot ýπÑý∏îýπâ

- **Modal Helpers (V.1.0, 2026-04-17)**: `[Admin System] DINOCO Modal Helpers` snippet. `window.dinocoModal.{confirm,alert,prompt}({})` API replacing native blocking dialogs. Scoped `.dnc-modal-*` CSS with ESC/focus-trap/backdrop-click support + native `confirm()/alert()/prompt()` fallback when snippet not loaded (defensive pattern via try/catch in callers). 6 destructive admin sites migrated in Phase 5: BO admin `bo_confirm_full`, `bo_reject`, `bo_cancel_item`, Split BO final confirm, B2F `rejectLot`, Phase 4 LIVE migration. ~67 `confirm/alert/prompt` sites remaining documented for Phase 6 bulk migration sprint.
- **Observability (V.1.0, 2026-04-17)**: `[Admin System] DINOCO Observability` snippet. 5 functions: `dinoco_obs_is_enabled($channel)`, `dinoco_obs_init_sentry()`, `dinoco_obs_capture($ex, $ctx)`, `dinoco_obs_get_request_id()`, + `rest_post_dispatch` filter injecting `X-Request-ID` correlation header on all DINOCO REST responses. 3 wp_option flags default=0: `dinoco_obs_sentry_enabled`, `dinoco_obs_correlation_enabled`, `dinoco_obs_structured_log`. Defensive `class_exists('\Sentry\Client')` check ‚Äî zero behavior change if SDK missing. Activation: `composer require sentry/sentry` + `DINOCO_SENTRY_DSN` env + flag flip. OpenClaw proxy V.2.1 adds optional `require('@sentry/node')` init gated by `process.env.SENTRY_DSN` (try/catch defensive).
- **GDPR Compliance (V.4.0, 2026-04-30)**: `[System] DINOCO GDPR Data Requests` snippet. Thai PDPA compliance ‚Äî full data export ZIP with cross-system MongoDB integration. Endpoints `POST /dinoco-gdpr/v1/my-data-export`, `POST /my-data-delete`, `GET /my-data-status` + admin review (V.3.0 Phase 7) at `/wp-json/dinoco-gdpr/v1/admin/*` ‚Äî all gated by `dinoco_gdpr_enabled` (default '0' ‚Üí 503 until activated). Schemas: `wp_dinoco_gdpr_requests` (15 cols incl. download_token + scope_json + cancellation_window_at + reviewed_by/at) + `wp_dinoco_gdpr_audit_log` (immutable trail per PDPA ¬ß39). **V.4.0 Round 26 LINE export**: NEW `dinoco_gdpr_export_line_messages($line_uid, $request_id)` ‚Äî calls OpenClaw agent (`agent:3000`) `GET /api/gdpr/line-messages` with bearer auth (`LIFF_AI_AGENT_KEY`), 10s timeout + 1 retry + Docker `agent:` ‚Üí `localhost:` fallback. Returns `{messages, claims, leads, total_count, generated_at, unavailable}`. Best-effort: agent unreachable ‚Üí `unavailable=true` ‚Üí adds `line-messages-UNAVAILABLE.txt` placeholder in ZIP (does NOT block rest of export). Cross-system audit: agent INSERT into MongoDB `gdpr_export_log` collection per call (rate limit 1/line_uid/hour). Data scope: wp_users + wp_usermeta + distributor CPT + warranties + claims + B2B orders + LINE conversation history via OpenClaw MongoDB. - **Idempotency-Key Helper + Endpoint Integration** (V.1.0, 2026-04-29, Rounds 18-40 ‚Äî üéØ 30% milestone reached Round 34, üéØ 40% milestone reached Round 38, üéØ 45% milestone reached Round 40 ‚Äî 89/196 = 45.4%): NEW `[Admin System] DINOCO Idempotency Helper` snippet (~600 LOC, additive infrastructure for safe POST retry handling ‚Äî closes audit memory `project_audit_2026_04_17_pending_actions.md` "API-H4" foundation). Schema `wp_dinoco_idempotency_keys` (lazy `dbDelta` on `admin_init`, idempotency_key VARCHAR(64) + namespace VARCHAR(64) + request_hash CHAR(64) + response_data LONGTEXT + response_code SMALLINT + user_id + request_ip + created_at + expires_at, 2 indexes: composite `idx_key_namespace` + `idx_expires_at`). 5 public functions all `function_exists` guarded: `dinoco_idempotency_hash($body)` SHA256 hex with body normalization, `dinoco_idempotency_extract_key($req)` strict header reader (1-64 chars `[A-Za-z0-9._-]` UUID/ULID compatible), `dinoco_idempotency_check($key, $namespace, $body)` returns array (replay) / WP_Error 409 (hash mismatch) / null (proceed), `dinoco_idempotency_store($key, $namespace, $body, $resp, $code, $ttl)` 24h replay TTL clamp 60s..7d, `dinoco_idempotency_query($args)` admin viewer. Cleanup cron `dinoco_idempotency_cleanup_cron` daily 03:15 chunked 1000/iter √ó 20 iter cap. REST API admin only `manage_options`+`wp_rest`: `GET /dinoco/v1/idempotency` + `POST /dinoco/v1/idempotency/cleanup`. Admin viewer shortcode `[dinoco_idempotency_viewer]`. **Endpoint integration progress (Round 34 ‚Äî üéØ 30.1% TRUE milestone, 59/196 POST endpoints ‚Äî first sustained crossing past 30%)**: 16 rounds (Round 19, 23, 25-34) batched 59 retry-prone POST endpoints across B2B (24) + B2F (19) + inventory (8) + MCP (7). Source of truth: [`docs/audit/IDEMPOTENCY-COVERAGE.md`](docs/audit/IDEMPOTENCY-COVERAGE.md). Round 30 REST endpoint census (`docs/audit/REST-ENDPOINT-CENSUS-2026-04-30.md`) established authoritative denominator of 193 POST endpoints ‚Äî earlier "% milestones" pre-Round 30 were against stale ~75 estimate (annotated in tracker). Round 19 founding 3: `POST /b2b/v1/place-order` (Snippet 3 V.42.10+) body hash `{gid, items, note, edit_ticket}` ‚Äî `edit_ticket` discriminates new vs edit retry; `POST /b2b/v1/manual-flash-create` body hash `{dst_*, item_desc, weight, sku, sender_key, dims}`; `POST /b2f/v1/create-po` (Snippet 2 V.11.11+) body hash `{user_id, maker_id, items, note, requested_date, exchange_rate, shipping_method}` ‚Äî different `exchange_rate` triggers 409 (DOUBLE-CHARGE prevention). Pattern (~50 LOC per endpoint, additive wrapper at top + bottom of handler): extract key (function_exists guard) ‚Üí compose body hash (semantic fields only, strip nonces/timestamps) ‚Üí check (409 / replay / null) ‚Üí run handler if null ‚Üí store before success return + `_idem_code` marker. Conflict response: HTTP 409 + `code: idempotency_conflict` + Thai user-facing message. Round 29 introduced `IdempotencyTestFixture` DRY base class (~80% LOC saved per test file). Round 30 fixed F1 drift bug (bo-fulfill listed integrated since Round 19 but had no wrapper). Round 31 added F1-class drift regression guard (`tests/jest/idempotency-tracker-drift.test.js`) ‚Äî parses tracker + asserts each claimed file contains `dinoco_idempotency_check` + endpoint suffix appears as string literal. Tests: `tests/helpers/IdempotencyTest.php` (foundation 25 cases) + `tests/helpers/IdempotencyEndpointContractTest.php` (Round 19-28 inline 20 cases) + 6 fixture-based round files (`IdempotencyRound29Test.php`/`Round30Test.php`/`Round31Test.php`/`Round32Test.php`/`Round33Test.php`/`Round34Test.php`) ‚Äî **236 cumulative contract tests** across Rounds 19-34. Backward compat: clients without `X-Idempotency-Key` header behave byte-identical pre-wrapper. **Future rounds**: 137 POST endpoints remaining (Round 33 census denominator 196). Round 35 high-priority candidates: dashboard-inject-metrics + lead-attribution + inventory-changed + kb-updated + product-compatibility (all MCP). 5 distinct patterns crystallized in `docs/patterns/IDEMPOTENCY-KEY.md` "Round 18-34 case study patterns" ‚Äî single / bulk / bulk-of-targets / state-machine / boolean-discriminator + enum-discriminator. 50% milestone (~98 endpoints) realistic timeline Round 50+.

G2 1003 (duplicate outTradeNo) recovery ‚Äî `b2b_flash_create_order_v42` $execute closure ý∏óý∏≥ 2-step: (1) idempotent recovery via `/open/v3/ordersByMchPno` query if Flash already accepted (network-lost ACK case), (2) regenerate `{ticket_id}-r{attempt}` suffix + sync subParcel.outTradeNo as fallback.     - **4 distinct root causes surfaced in iteration**:
      1. **Status labels drift** (V.3.13, `5765470`): Snippet 1 `b2b_get_status_labels()` ý∏Çý∏≤ý∏î `'pending_stock_review'` + `'partial_fulfilled'` (ýπÄý∏ûý∏¥ýπàý∏°ýπÉý∏ô FSM V.1.6 ýπÄý∏°.ý∏¢. 2026 ýπÅý∏ïýπàý∏•ý∏∑ý∏° sync ýπÄý∏Çýπâý∏≤ Snippet 1 labels list).
      2. **FSM transition rejected ‚Äî `$actor` arg discarded**: `b2b_set_order_status($ticket_id, $new_status)` ý∏£ý∏±ý∏öýπÅý∏Ñýπà 2 args ýπÅý∏ïýπà caller ý∏™ýπàý∏á 3 (Snippet 2:910 + Snippet 3:1317 ý∏™ýπàý∏á `actor='customer'`) ‚Üí arg ý∏ñý∏πý∏Å discard.       3. **LINE Flex schema HTTP 400** (V.3.16, `6fcf530`): footer button "ý∏¢ý∏∑ý∏ôý∏¢ý∏±ý∏ôýπÄý∏ïýπáý∏°" used `'color' => $insufficient > 0 ? null : '#10b981'` ‚Üí LINE Flex schema: `button.color` must be hex string or KEY MUST BE OMITTED.     - **V.3.23 üî¥ double-debt regression fix** (`557523e`): fullstack-developer FINAL verification caught BLOCKER-1 from V.34.33: bo-split ‚Üí `debt_add(confirmed_value=ý∏ø5,000)` ‚úì + `is_billed=FALSE` ‚Üí customer Flex partial_fulfill ‚Üí customer "ý∏¢ý∏∑ý∏ôý∏¢ý∏±ý∏ôý∏öý∏¥ý∏•" ‚Üí `b2b_action_confirm_bill` checks `$was_billed=false` ‚Üí `b2b_debt_add(total_amount=ý∏ø8,000)` ‚ùå ‚Üí ý∏ïý∏±ý∏ßýπÅý∏óý∏ôý∏´ý∏ôý∏µýπâ ý∏ø13,000 (ý∏àý∏£ý∏¥ý∏áý∏Ñý∏ßý∏£ýπÄý∏õýπáý∏ô ý∏ø5,000) ‚Üí finance dashboard ýπÄý∏ûý∏µýπâý∏¢ý∏ô. Root cause: bo-split + bo-fulfill both add debt but never set `is_billed=true` ‚Üí confirm_bill doesn't know debt was added ‚Üí adds again. **Fix: bo-split + bo-fulfill atomic-set `is_billed=true` alongside debt_add**.
    - **V.3.24 + V.3.25 FULL REDESIGN** (`459c6fe` + `6c112bf`): Boss "Flex ý∏´ýπâý∏≠ý∏áýπÅý∏≠ý∏îý∏°ý∏¥ý∏ôýπÑý∏°ýπàý∏•ý∏∞ýπÄý∏≠ý∏µý∏¢ý∏îý∏ûý∏≠ý∏àý∏∞ýπÄý∏äýπáý∏Ñý∏Çý∏≠ý∏á" + "ý∏Ñý∏ßý∏£ý∏°ý∏µý∏£ý∏πý∏õý∏™ý∏¥ý∏ôý∏Ñýπâý∏≤ ý∏àý∏≥ý∏ôý∏ßý∏ôýπÉý∏´ýπâýπÄý∏îýπàý∏ô" + "ýπÑý∏°ýπàý∏ïýπâý∏≠ý∏áý∏°ý∏µ % ý∏™ýπàý∏ßý∏ôý∏•ý∏î" + "ýπÑý∏°ýπàý∏ïýπâý∏≠ý∏áý∏°ý∏µý∏¢ý∏≠ý∏îýπÄý∏áý∏¥ý∏ô ý∏Çýπâý∏≤ý∏áý∏´ý∏•ý∏±ý∏á" + "ý∏°ý∏µýπÅý∏Ñýπàý∏¢ý∏≠ý∏îý∏£ý∏ßý∏°ýπÅý∏öý∏öýπÄý∏îý∏¥ý∏°ý∏îý∏µýπÅý∏•ýπâý∏ß" ‚Üí ux-ui-expert role-based information architecture: **Admin Flex = operational** (ý∏îý∏πý∏Çý∏≠ý∏á ý∏ïý∏±ý∏îý∏™ý∏¥ý∏ôýπÉý∏à split/confirm/reject) ‚Äî ýπÑý∏°ýπàýπÄý∏´ýπáý∏ôý∏£ý∏≤ý∏Ñý∏≤/ý∏™ýπàý∏ßý∏ôý∏•ý∏î vs **Customer Flex = financial** (ý∏¢ý∏≠ý∏îýπÄý∏áý∏¥ý∏ô ETA ý∏ßý∏¥ý∏òý∏µý∏àýπàý∏≤ý∏¢) ‚Äî ýπÑý∏°ýπàýπÄý∏´ýπáý∏ôý∏™ý∏ïýπáý∏≠ý∏Å/SKU ýπÄý∏õý∏•ýπàý∏≤.     - **Lessons**:
      1. Boss UX iteration speed-of-iteration beats up-front design when business is wedged ‚Äî 13 commits in one day driven by 6 distinct boss screenshots.
      2. Schema-validation Flex bugs (null color) only surface at LINE API runtime ‚Äî push retry queue + GAVE UP alert is essential for diagnosis.
      3. State machines touching debt MUST atomic-set `is_billed=true` alongside `debt_add()` ‚Äî V.3.23 regression came from V.34.33 fix that didn't update flag.
      4. `all_backorder` vs `partial_fulfilled` = product distinction. Customer experience differs fundamentally: partial = "ý∏¢ý∏∑ý∏ôý∏¢ý∏±ý∏ôý∏öý∏¥ý∏• now"; all = "ý∏¢ý∏ÅýπÄý∏•ý∏¥ý∏ÅýπÑý∏îýπâý∏ïý∏•ý∏≠ý∏î until ý∏Çý∏≠ý∏áý∏°ý∏≤".
  - **S/N Round 11 Deep Audit** (2026-05-12 R11, commits `8d625a3` + `1475a8d`): 1 BLOCKER + 2 HIGH closed via R11 code-reviewer agent hunt on 8 NEW categories R1-R10 did NOT cover. **BLOCKER-1 ‚Äî `dinoco_obs_capture()` signature drift (54 sites √ó 8 files)**: All call sites passed Throwable / null / `new \Exception(...)` as FIRST arg to `dinoco_obs_capture($level, $message, $context)`. Defensive coercion in Observability snippet (`is_string($level)` ‚Üí 'info' fallback + `wp_json_encode($message)`) swallowed exception class+message+stack as literal `{}` log payload. **Production impact**: since SN launched 2026-05-04, ALL sensitive ops (batch_create / void / swap / recall / reissue / stolen_report / marketplace refund / claim sync / 13+ cron handlers) had ZERO exception telemetry. Invisible to Sentry, error_log, structured logs. **Fix**: 49 sed renames + 5 targeted Edits (Throwable `$te` SN REST:6127 / `$geo_e` Warranty LIFF:1685 / `new \Exception(...)` SN Manager:1368 + 1408 / wrapper helper `dinoco_sn_obs_capture` `null, $payload` ‚Üí `'info', $tag, $payload`). 8 snippets bumped (SN Approval V.0.1‚ÜíV.0.2 / SN REST API V.0.41‚ÜíV.0.42 / SN Manager V.0.55‚ÜíV.0.56 / SN Reconciliation V.0.2‚ÜíV.0.3 / Public API Gateway V.0.3‚ÜíV.0.4 / Service Center V.31.5‚ÜíV.31.6 / Warranty Activation LIFF V.0.17‚ÜíV.0.18 / Manual Transfer V.31.3‚ÜíV.31.4). **HIGH-2 ‚Äî `dinoco_sn_pool_stats_v1` cache invalidation**: 60s admin Tab 3 cache missed from R3 cache invalidation chain ‚Üí activate/void/recall/swap left counts stale. Fix: NEW listener `dinoco_sn_invalidate_pool_stats_cache` @ priority 6 (SN REST API V.0.43). **HIGH-3 ‚Äî LTV transient never invalidated on cron UPSERT**: 1hr per-user tier badge cache. Daily cron `dinoco_sn_run_ltv_snapshot` UPSERTs but never `delete_transient` ‚Üí tier downgrade stuck up to 1hr. Fix: `delete_transient('dinoco_sn_ltv_' . $user_id)` inside cron loop after each `ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE` (SN Manager V.0.57). **R11 drift detectors (13 NEW Jest assertions)**: per-file Throwable-call scan √ó 8 + new-Exception variant + wrapper signature + Observability function definition + pool_stats listener wired + LTV cron invalidation. **Critical lesson**: strip PHP comment lines BEFORE regex scan ‚Äî version headers contain literal "dinoco_obs_capture( $e, ... )" describing the fix, would self-trigger false-positive otherwise.

Sites: `dinoco_sn_run_marketplace_timeout` (lines 10227 + 10260) + `dinoco_sn_run_pool_stats_recompute` (line 12392). **Category A defense (8 sites ‚Äî HIGH)**: heartbeat OUTSIDE try/catch but vulnerable to catch-block re-throw.     1. Boss screenshot feedback is the highest-fidelity UX signal ‚Äî 3-4 iteration cycles are normal; past 8 rounds means a fundamental issue (cache / asset / cascade), not pixel tuning.

## üßÝ Second Brain Integration

repo ý∏ôý∏µýπâýπÄý∏äý∏∑ýπàý∏≠ý∏°ý∏Åý∏±ý∏ö central knowledge wiki ý∏óý∏µýπà `.second-brain/`
(symlink ýπÑý∏õý∏óý∏µýπà `~/Projects/second-brain/wiki/`, gitignored)
